Only the chauffeur, Toshio Oki, was apprehended after the 15th. On the surface, it seemed that the case could be considered closed with the arrest of the four criminals, and everything would return to normal (the stolen 31,000+ yuan was taken by the Communist Party). However, in reality, even the official authorities consider the matter extremely serious. First and foremost, it is a matter of thought. The widespread clandestine movement of communist organizations and the source of the weapons they use warrant careful attention.

Amid economic turmoil and Japan's active military aggression in China, the general atmosphere is uniformly militaristic. Not only are leftist ideas forbidden from developing, but even liberal thinkers like Kijūrō Shidehara (Minister of Foreign Affairs during the Wakatsuki Cabinet during the September 18th Incident) were placed on a black list for assassination by the ["Blood Brotherhood"]. Yet, the Communist Party, which is extremely leftist, dares to disregard the law and conduct clandestine movements, and it is doing so very quickly. Many people in society sympathize with them, especially with their opposition to imperialist aggression. In the past, this was merely a thought movement; practical actions were limited to lectures among workers and the formation of labor unions and political parties. In the past half-year, however, the nature of the movement has changed. For example, after the robbery of the Kawasaki Daihyaku Bank this time, searches of related locations turned up over thirty pistols and box cannons, and approximately eight thousand rounds of ammunition. This is an unprecedented and terrible incident in Japan. Although it is not a direct political or economic problem, the source of such guns and ammunition in a militaristic and well-organized society is worth examining in detail (Tokyo, October 16, 1932).

Sichuan War Expanding Daily 79

Liu Xiang's Troops Garrisoned in Hubei Prepare to Continue Operations in Sichuan

Wuhan University Students from Sichuan Telegraph Pleas to Cease Conflict and Resist Foreign Enemies

Hankou Correspondence. The unfortunate Sichuan war has erupted at a time when national crisis is imminent. According to telegrams from Sichuan, intense fighting has broken out between the two sides of Qing Shun. The situation is tense throughout Eastern Sichuan, and the situation is likely to escalate. Guo Xun's brigade of Liu Xiang's troops stationed in Hubei, which was previously ordered to return to Sichuan, has now joined the operations in Shunqing. The area around Jingzhou and Shashi is being defended by Liu Guangyu's brigade of the Second Division. Fan Shaozeng's troops of the Fourth Division, which are also a strong force for suppressing bandits in Hubei, have reportedly been recalled from the front line to concentrate in Jingzhou and Shashi, with talk of continuing into Sichuan. The tension in Sichuan is evident. When the two Lius came into contact, the second-tier generals of Sichuan sent a joint telegram proposing to convene a Suining Conference to resolve the Sichuan situation. Deng Xihou, Liu Cunhou, Yang Sen, Tian Songyao, etc., have recently expressed their agreement, and response telegrams have been arriving in Hankou continuously. On the surface, everyone hopes for peace, but whether this is truly the case is uncertain. The generals of Sichuan each have their own agendas, and the mutual restraint of the two Lius is welcomed by Deng, Liu, Yang, and Tian. Sichuan natives in Hankou are deeply aware of the complexity of the Sichuan situation and hold many anxieties. On the 21st, Sichuan students at National Wuhan University telegraphed all parties, urging them to cease conflict and resist foreign enemies, and not to harm the country and its people. The original telegram reads as follows: [To Commander Liu of Chongqing, Commander Liu of Chengdu, Commander Deng, Commander Tian of Santai, Commander Yang of Guang'an, Sichuan citizens have suffered from war for a long time and are tired of war. For the past twenty years, chaos has followed chaos, and bandits are rampant. The land once known as the "Land of Abundance" is now a "Realm of Ghosts." Why is Heaven so unkind to Sichuan? You, gentlemen, have received the generous support of your hometown and the affection of your elders. You hold the power to balance and wield the authority to command. Raising your arms and shouting would surely be enough to reverse the declining situation and illuminate the future. Our expectations are no more urgent than this. Moreover, since the national crisis occurred last year, the divine land has been sinking. To save the nation, we must first save ourselves. Fortunately, the military and political leaders of all provinces are able to unite sincerely to seek renewal, and the general public is also working to survive. At this time, owls are crying on the branches, thinking of spying on our homes. There should be no internal strife, and no one should be a leader of national harm. You, gentlemen, have started wars for private interests, regardless of the nation's survival. The bad news has arrived, and we are filled with fear and anxiety. For your sake, the best option is to request permission to kill the enemy, fulfill the military's duty to defend the country, and avenge old grievances. The second best is to cultivate and educate, repay the support of the people, and build a new nation. If you indulge in temporary pleasure and disregard the condemnation of future generations, pursue personal gains, and disregard the nation's peril, that is the worst, and you, gentlemen, should despise and scorn it even more. Our association cares about our homeland and cannot bear to see the villages in ruins. We advocate the gentlemanly virtue of loving others with virtue and look forward to your great achievements. We have presented everything in detail and hope you will understand clearly. We hope that you will cherish yourselves and love others and not become a laughingstock to the world. Our hearts are tormented, and we cannot express all that we want to say. The Sichuan Students Association of National Wuhan University bows. ] (October 21st)

Hubei Province Reduces Administration Again 80

Hankou Correspondence. Hubei Province's financial difficulties have reached an extreme. Monthly revenue is only 1.2 million yuan, while expenditure reaches 1.9 million yuan, leaving a shortfall of over 700,000 yuan. The Commander-in-Chief of Bandit Suppression sent personnel to investigate earlier this month, confirming a plan for reorganization. He instructed the provincial government to strictly implement austerity measures and stipulated that the total amount of administrative expenses each month should not exceed 700,000 yuan. He ordered the revision of the new budget for the 21st year of the Republic, to be implemented from October 1st. After receiving the order, the provincial government consulted with its affiliated agencies and decided to cut what should be cut, reduce what should be reduced, and merge what should be merged. After spending a long time, the new budget was drafted and submitted to the headquarters for review. After being reviewed by Jia Shiyi, who was designated by the headquarters to be responsible for the review, it has been completed. However, the monthly expenditure of the new budget is still over 800,000 yuan, which is far from the stipulated amount of 700,000 yuan. Therefore, the provincial government was instructed to re-compile the budget, and detailed instructions were also given on the points that should be cut and reduced. The provincial government put forward the 46th meeting for discussion on the 21st, and decided to follow the order to reduce further. It is reported that no fewer than ten agencies will be cut or merged, such as the Autonomous Preparatory Committee, the Provincial Hospital, the Public Property Clearing Office, the Debt Donation Office, the Police Academy, the Wuhan Ferry Office, the Provincial Wireless Radio Station, and the Music Corps. They will either be merged into the Civil Affairs, Finance, and Construction Departments, or be shut down altogether. The departments themselves are also economizing, and all incompetent personnel will be dismissed. In order to clarify the significance of cutting expenses, the headquarters re-ordered the provincial government on the 21st, stating that the most important significance of the headquarters' order to cut various expenses in the province this time is, on the one hand, to maintain the province's financial resources so that they will not fall into the danger of provincial financial bankruptcy due to increasing accumulated deficits. On the other hand, it is to obtain satisfactory administrative efficiency with appropriate financial resources. Therefore, agencies that can be cut and abolished should be cut and abolished, and those that can be merged should be merged. However, the headquarters does not advocate for a universal reduction of the items listed, so that the amount of salary each person receives is too low, causing employees to experience difficulties in life and reducing work efficiency. The provincial government should immediately, based on this meaning, strictly assess the civil servants of its own agencies and affiliated agencies, and immediately implement the dismissal of those who are redundant or have low capabilities. The quantity should be approximately the same as the quantity of public officials' original salaries, so that employees can still receive considerable salaries after the budget reduction and will not be disheartened and distracted due to low salaries. It is expected that the result of the austerity measures of the agencies this time will be to reduce personnel without reducing salaries (October 21st).

The Zheng Jicheng Case Has Been Judged 81

Zheng Sentenced to Seven Years, Will Appeal

Full Text of the Judgment Released

Jinan Correspondence: Zhang Zongchang arrived in Jinan from Beijing on September 2nd, stating his intention to return to his hometown of Ye County, but was unsuccessful. On the afternoon of the 3rd, he hastily returned to Beijing. At the Jinan Railway Station, Zheng Jicheng, the nephew of Zheng Jinsheng, who was previously killed by Zhang, and his follower Chen Fengshan, ambushed and killed him. At the same time, Zhang's bodyguard, Liu Huaizhou, was also shot and killed, and Liu Qingxun was injured. Zheng immediately declared that he was avenging his uncle and surrendered to the station's law enforcement team. He was subsequently detained in the military court of the Third Route Army Headquarters. This incident caused a nationwide sensation. Many people inside and outside the province considered Zheng's actions righteous and requested the government to pardon him. On the 24th of last month, the provincial government, following orders from the central government, transferred Zheng to the Jinan District Court. After several investigations by prosecutors Zhu Weiran and Zhu Fengxiang, a public prosecution was filed. The District Court held a public hearing on the 15th of this month. After the debate concluded, the verdict was announced yesterday (the 19th). Zheng was sentenced to seven years of imprisonment for premeditated murder. The full text of the judgment, comprising over 2,500 characters, was transcribed and verified, and released today. It is reported that local groups have prepared to petition the central government for amnesty under the amnesty regulations, granting Zheng a special pardon, so that both law and human sentiment can be considered. I visited Zheng in the court detention center today and asked him what his opinion was on the court's judgment. Zheng said that he had no objections to the judgment, but someone is currently telegraphing the central government to request a special pardon for him. The exchange of telegrams will take some time, and the deadline for appealing the judgment is only ten days, which will be reached in the blink of an eye. He fears that the special pardon will not be granted before the ten-day deadline expires, thus losing the opportunity to appeal. Therefore, he has decided to first appeal to the Shandong High Court, contesting the point of premeditated murder. He has already asked a lawyer to draft the appeal today, and so on. The court's judgment is recorded below for those concerned about this case to browse.

Jinan District Court Criminal First Instance Judgment (21st Year Di Zi No. 141) Defendant Zheng Jicheng, male, age 40, Licheng native, residing at No. 7 Bianzhi Lane, Jinan City. Appointed defense lawyers: Zhou Qingen, Sun Baifu, Li Yunsheng. The right defendant, due to the murder case, was publicly prosecuted by the prosecutor of this court. This court sentences as follows: Main Text: Zheng Jicheng is sentenced to seven years of imprisonment for premeditated murder, deprived of civil rights for seven years. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized will be used to offset the sentence at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. Two pistols, twenty-eight bullets, and one bullet head are all confiscated.

Facts: The defendant, Zheng Jicheng, is the stepson of the former Deputy Commander of the Eighth Route Army, Zheng Jinsheng. Because Zheng Jinsheng was murdered by the former Shandong Military Governor Zhang Zongchang in the 16th year of the Republic of China, he held a grudge in his heart. On September 2nd of this year, Zhang Zongchang, along with his bodyguards Liu Huaizhou (i.e., Liu Huaizhou), Liu Qingxun, Xia Tingfang, and others, came to Jinan from Beijing and resided at the Shi Gongguan on Weiyi Road. At 3 p.m. the next day, Zheng Jicheng returned home from the Charity Association and heard that Zhang Zongchang and others would return to Beijing that day. At around 5 p.m., while eating at home, he thought of the old feud and conceived the intention to kill him. He telephoned the Shi Gongguan to inquire and learned that Zhang Zongchang and others had already departed, believing that this was an opportunity not to be missed. Before finishing his meal, he arranged with the fugitive Chen Fengshan, each carrying a pistol. Zheng Jicheng carried twenty-eight bullets, and Fengshan carried six bullets. They took a car to the Shi Gongguan on Weiyi Road, but found the door closed and no car, assuming that Zhang Zongchang and others had indeed gone to the station. They rushed to the Jinpu Railway Jinan Railway Station. At that time, the northbound train was stopped on the third track of the second platform. Zheng Jicheng and Chen Fengshan mingled into the crowd of people seeing them off. Zhang Zongchang came out of the first-class carriage to see off guests. Zheng Jicheng and Chen Fengshan raised their guns to shoot, but the bullets did not fire. Zhang Zongchang caught a glimpse of them and turned to avoid them, jumping down from the east end of the carriage and fleeing northeast. Zheng Jicheng and Chen Fengshan pursued him. Liu Huaizhou and Liu Qingxun rushed to protect him and were shot by Zheng Jicheng and Chen Fengshan, hitting Zhang Zongchang and Liu Huaizhou in vital parts, causing them to fall to the ground and die instantly. Liu Qingxun was also shot and injured. After treatment, he was fortunate enough to survive. Because the station was in chaos at the time, Zheng Jicheng surrendered to the station's law enforcement team of the Third Route Army Headquarters before the military police discovered the crime, requesting to be handed over to the official authorities for judgment. The military court transferred the case to the Shandong Provincial Government, which handed over Zheng Jicheng to this court. The prosecutor completed the investigation and filed a public prosecution.

Reasons: The main points of the prosecution's indictment are roughly as follows: After investigating, the defendant, Zheng Jicheng, and the fugitive, Chen Fengshan, harbored resentment for a long time because Zheng Jinsheng was killed by Zhang Zongchang. This time, they carried pistols and took a car to the station to commit the crime, which was premeditated. However, with a single general intent, at the same time and place, committing one act to kill three people, according to Article 42 of the Criminal Law, each constitutes a crime under Article 284, paragraph 1, item 1, and paragraph 2 of the same law, which is equivalent to the provisions of the first part of Article 74 of the same law, and should be punished according to the more serious crime. Furthermore, the defendant surrendered to the law enforcement team before the crime was discovered, which may reduce the penalty for the first crime by one-third. Moreover, the circumstances of the crime are excusable and may be reduced at the discretion of the court in accordance with Article 77 of the same law, and so on.

The main points of the defense are roughly as follows: Premeditated murder requires a long period of preparation and planning. The defendant's intention to kill Zhang Zongchang arose after returning home from the Charity Association to drink alcohol and before 6:10 p.m. when he took a car to the station. The time elapsed from the time when Zheng conceived the intention to avenge his uncle to the time when Zhang was killed was not more than half an hour. The intent to avenge his uncle was only revealed to Chen Fengshan as the car approached the station. Therefore, it cannot be said that it was premeditated murder. Moreover, a bullet was recovered from the body of the deceased Liu Huaizhou, which was definitely not a bullet from the box-type gun carried by the defendant, which is sufficient to prove that Liu Huaizhou and Liu Qingxun were not killed by the defendant. Chen Fengshan accompanied him to the station only for protection. The defendant did not order him to shoot and bombard. Even if the death and injury of Liu Huaizhou and others were the result of Chen Fengshan's crime, the defendant was unaware of this and could not foresee this fact, and should not bear joint criminal responsibility, and so on. (To be continued)

Ministry of Interior Sends Personnel to Inspect the Yellow River 82

Wang Yingyu Discusses River Management Opinions

Jinan Correspondence: The Yellow River has been a frequent disaster in recent years, with Shandong and Henan provinces, located at the lower reaches, suffering the most. The Ministry of Interior believes that to fundamentally manage the river, it is necessary to conduct a detailed investigation of the entire river, so it has specially sent Wang Yingyu, a member of the Water Conservancy Commission, to Shandong to first inspect the lowest reaches of the Yellow River where it enters the sea, and then go upstream to inspect the entire river. Wang arrived in Jinan on the 14th, contacted the Shandong River Affairs Bureau on the 15th, and departed from Jinan on the 16th. The River Affairs Bureau sent Pan Yifen, head of the Engineering Section, and Wang Baichen, secretary, to accompany him. Qiang Hanying, president of the Jinan branch of the Engineering Society, also accompanied them. On the morning of the 16th, the group of four traveled by car from Jinan City to Luokou and boarded a boat, going downstream. They stayed overnight in Qinghe Town that night, arrived at Wang Wangzhuang on the 17th, and arrived at Lijin on the 18th. They observed and inquired along the way, with Pan providing explanations and exchanging opinions. They also carefully inspected the shape of the estuary and summoned local elders to inquire about the past water conditions and the gains and losses of defense methods. On the 19th, they returned to Jinan by car from Lijin. That evening, the River Affairs Bureau hosted a public banquet for Wang Yingyu, with Liang Shuming from the Rural Construction Research Institute also attending. It was decided that tomorrow (the 21st) they would take a car from Jinan to inspect Lisherg Dun and other places upstream, following the route into Henan Province, with Pan Yifen and Zhang Hanying accompanying them. Pan will go as far as the Shandong border, while Zhang is scheduled to go to Mengjin for inspection. According to Wang's discussion of the inspection situation and river management opinions, [the relationship between the estuary and the upper reaches is the most important for river management. This inspection of the lower reaches shows that the estuary of Lijin has no bunds to bind it, the water is shallow and the flow is slow, and the scouring force is small, resulting in more and more siltation at the estuary and boundless reeds, which impede the water flow and make breaches most likely. My opinion on the lower reaches is to add dikes until the estuary to bind the river water and to remove the reeds to smooth the water flow. Moreover, according to the locals, historically, there have never been breaches at places where there are stone dams on the entire river, which shows the importance of stone dams. To avoid breaches, the only way is to build stone dams on the entire river. This matter does not seem to be as difficult as imagined in managing the Yellow River, but stone dams cost the most. The government is unable to provide subsidies, and it is not easy for local areas to raise funds. An investigation shows that there are 4 million mu of silted land in Lijin downstream. If immigrants cultivate the land, the minimum income per mu per year is one yuan, which is 4 million yuan a year. If this money is saved to build stone dams, it can be completed in a few years. If the government can provide subsidies, success will be even faster. If immigrants cultivate the land, the most important things are (1) harassment by sea bandits, (2) seawater cannot be drunk, and other drinks must be prepared, and (3) transportation must be planned in advance. In the future, as the water force increases, Tianjin and Yantai will not be far away, steamships can enter the port, and the estuary can become an important town. To regulate the river water, a reservoir lake should be built in the upper reaches, which requires a lot of land, and the people can be moved to the lower reaches to cultivate the land, so they will not lose their jobs. Regarding the middle reaches, in Henan, I once inspected it in a private capacity. The river channel seems to be too wide. In the future, ways can be found to narrow it slightly. However, the greatest harm of the Yellow River lies in carrying sediment. Ways must be found to reduce the sediment. There is a river in the upper reaches of Gansu, Bird and Mouse Mountain, the source of the Wei River, which is blocked by Bird and Mouse Mountain and flows north into the Yellow River. If the river is diverted into the Wei River, the water force of the Yellow River will be smaller, so less sediment will be carried out when it reaches the Hetao area, and more branch canals will be opened in the Hetao area to irrigate the fields, so as to discharge the water force and sediment. Then the sediment in the Yellow River will be less in the future. At the same time, the Wei River will become a clear stream. As it adds tributaries, the water force will naturally be greater. After entering the Yellow River, the force of scouring sediment will also be greater. The silting will be lighter, the water flow will be smoother, and the danger of breaches may be reduced. ] (October 20th)

Kong Hechong's Bandits Disturb Jing'an 83

Have Been Dispersed by Luo Lin's Troops

Nanchang Correspondence: According to military sources, after the bandit Kong Hechong fled from the southeast of Hubei Province to the northwest of Jiangxi Province, they initially fiercely attacked Ruichang, Wu'ning, Xiushui, and Tonggu counties. Because the stationed troops were prepared, they were unsuccessful. They then turned to disturb Wanzai, Yichun, Yifeng, and Fenyi. They were also repelled due to the strong defense of the stationed troops. Recently, in order to avoid the strong and attack the weak, the bandits sent the 9th Regiment of the pseudo-16th Army to sneak into Jing'an via Xiushui. According to a letter from Jing'an, at 3 a.m. on the 9th of this month, the county government received an urgent report from the Fourth District Office that more than a thousand bandits had arrived at Xitou. At about 7 a.m., the bandits had fled to Hegang. There were more than a thousand bandits, with four to five hundred guns, two machine guns, and the rest were stretcher teams with carrying poles and ropes. When they first arrived, they first went to the Fox Tail Ridge heights west of the city, and another group fired dozens of shots, swarming into the city and searching and looting separately. They arrested anyone they met. At this time, a reconnaissance plane flew in from the province. The bandits hid in houses or under the eaves. After the plane left, they looted as before. On the morning of the 10th, the bandits transported the looted property, three to four hundred loads, and more than a hundred hostages, to Renci Mountain, five miles from the city. In the morning, a fighter plane also arrived and fired fiercely at the bandits with machine guns at low altitude. The bandits mostly hid in the grass, mountains, forests, eaves, and corners of houses. After three or four hours, the plane flew away, and the bandits came out again to burn and plunder wantonly. That night, the bandits sat in the county government hall and dragged the hostages to be tortured to extort money. Tang Daqing, an alternate member of the Fourth District Party Department, was beheaded and chopped into four pieces. The bandits, having emptied the essence of the county, retreated to the northwest on the 11th. The first security team immediately entered the city and restored order. When the bandits captured Jing'an, the headquarters of the three provinces telegraphed Luo Lin, Yue Sen, Liu Yi, and other troops to surround the bandits in Jing'an. After receiving the order, Luo's troops immediately dispatched Chen Youpeng's regiment to Hegang, Tang's regiment to Nanping Bridge, and another regiment to guard the junction of Xiushui, Wu'ning, Jing'an, and Fengxin, cutting off the bandits' retreat to their old lair. Chen's regiment encountered the bandits in Hegang on the 11th. After several hours of fighting, two hundred bandits were killed, dozens were captured alive, and more than twenty hostages were rescued. The bandits then collapsed from Lion Cliff towards Xiushui. Chen's regiment anticipated that the bandits would detour to Nanping Bridge and took the road to Baisha Bridge to intercept them. On the morning of the 12th, they encountered the bandits again. Chen's regiment fought bravely, and more than half of the bandits were killed or wounded. More than a hundred rifles were seized, and the four hundred loads of property looted by the bandits and more than a hundred hostages were all intercepted. The remnants of the bandits fled towards Madong Zhusha'ao. At this time, Tang's regiment also arrived and joined the search and suppression in Baimao, in order to annihilate the remnants. (October 16th)

Shantou Strictly Prohibits Silver Exports 84

The Municipal Government Has an Existing Ban

The Customs Administration Actually Issued Passports

The Public Security Bureau Cracked a Case

Shantou Correspondence: Because it is profitable to export silver dollars to Shanghai, silver exchange shops in this city are willing to destabilize the city's finances and collude with a certain maritime agency to smuggle silver exports. Each thousand yuan can earn a net profit of more than forty yuan, resulting in chaotic finances in the market for several days. Moreover, each silver shop takes advantage of the opportunity of silver shortage (Shantou banknotes cannot be used across borders) when merchants need to borrow interest money from silver shops between autumn and winter to purchase goods from other places, increasing the interest rate and exchange rate. The Shantou Chamber of Commerce is extremely dissatisfied with the heavy exploitation of merchants by silver shops. In order to save finances, it specially convened a meeting on the 17th and resolved to request the government to reiterate the ban on silver exports, and also notified the exchange silver industry and the two guilds to study proper measures to maintain the market. Therefore, the municipal government also issued a notice that each person is only allowed to bring fifty yuan of silver dollars or small coins for export. Those who exceed the limit and export privately minted silver bars will be treated as smuggling, detained and confiscated, and the police team is not allowed to accept bribes and release them. Moreover, the detective team of the Public Security Bureau received a report from an informant yesterday that a Hao firm was privately shipping silver to Shanghai ships, totaling twenty-four boxes, each box containing five thousand yuan. When they were being transferred to barges to be loaded onto the ships, they were seized by the Public Security Bureau. At the same time, the Customs also sent customs officers to investigate. The Public Security Bureau sent additional security teams to supervise. Of the twenty-four boxes, seven boxes were small coins, and those with passports issued by the Customs Supervisory Office were detained by the Customs, and the rest were taken away by the Public Security Bureau. The firms transporting silver exports were: Yun Da, sent two boxes to Chen Yuanda in Shanghai (this firm was opened by Chen Daonan, chairman of the Shantou Chamber of Commerce); Guanghua, sent four boxes to Puyi in Shanghai; Yongli, sent seven boxes to Puyi; Xiexing, sent three boxes to Nanhua in Shanghai; Maoxing, sent five boxes to Jiesheng in Shanghai, and Zhizhi, sent three boxes. There were also shipments to Yitai, Baoda, and Puyi. Among them, those who had already obtained customs passports were: Maoxing three boxes, Yongli two boxes, and Zhizhi three boxes. Each box contained five thousand yuan. After being transported to Shanghai, each box could earn a profit of two hundred yuan. Now that they have been intercepted, they may be confiscated by the government.

Hunan Province Successfully Tests Coal-Powered Automobiles 85

Long-Distance and Short-Distance Tests Conducted More Than Twenty Times

Trial Results with Charcoal Burning are Excellent

Changsha Correspondence: Xiang De, a technician of the Hunan Construction Department, and Liu Min, a section chief, have successfully tested coal-powered automobiles after six months of research. On October 11th, representatives specially sent by the four ministries of Industry, Railways, Military Administration, and General Staff, as well as representatives from thirteen provinces including Guizhou, Guizhou, Hubei, Henan, Zhili, Shanxi, Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Jiangxi, Shandong, Gansu, Fujian, and Qinghai, totaling forty-eight people, and foreign guests visiting Hunan, including Mr. and Mrs. An Lide, the American consul in China, and news media including Xu Chen, Yuan Qingming, and a reporter delegation from various Hankou newspapers, and a Hankou bank group, etc., from the 11th to the 15th, successively conducted one long-distance test drive, from Changsha to Yiyang, a round trip of 400 li, taking only five hours, and the results were extremely satisfactory. As for short-distance test drives, there were no less than twenty times. Because the representatives went to various construction agencies, famous scenic spots, and various banquets in the coal-powered automobiles in the past few days, their speed and comfort were comparable to gasoline-powered cars. On the 16th, Pi Zuoqiong, a special representative of the Ministry of Industry, convened representatives from various provinces, experts, and conducted the final long-distance test drive, and made a record as the general result of Hunan Province's trial of coal-powered automobiles. The route

Page 10

was from Changsha to Xiangtan. The results were as good as the first long-distance test drive, and it was a complete success. On the 17th, representatives from the central government and various provinces and experts held a meeting and decided to organize the [China Coal Gas Power Research Society], with Tan Changkai as the president, Liu Min as the chief executive of the administrative department, and Xiang De as the chief executive of the research department. It was decided that the first annual meeting will be held in Nanjing on the Double Tenth Festival in the 22nd year, and a special issue will be published, welcoming scholars and experts from all over the country who study coal gas power to join as members, and jointly study all the progress and improvement matters of coal-powered automobiles. Now that the trial is over, all the representatives have left Hunan on the 18th. The records of the last long-distance test drive from Changsha to Xiangtan will be recorded below to show the achievements of the test drive in Zhou Province. Explanation of the coal gas generator (A) Type: Suction-type generator, consisting of the first cleaner, the second cleaner, and the regulator. (B) Weight: Without charcoal and cleaning filter materials, it weighs 715 pounds. With cleaning filter materials, it weighs a total of 782 pounds (using charcoal and wood as cleaning filter materials). (C) Fuel: Charcoal, each piece about one inch in size. (D) Cleaning filter materials: The first cleaner uses coke and wood fiber as cleaning filter materials, and the second cleaner uses oil-soaked wood fiber and sawdust as cleaning filter materials. (E) Main dimensions: The generator has a diameter of 18 inches and a total height of 74 inches. The first cleaner has a diameter of 15 inches and a total height of 60 inches. The second cleaner is 48 inches long, 12 inches wide, and 10.5 inches high. The inner diameter of the air pipe, gas pipe, and mixed gas pipe of the regulator are all 2 inches. The diameter of the gas guide pipe (purple pipe and rubber pipe) is 4 inches, and the diameter of the air inlet pipe is 3 inches. (F) Charcoal capacity: 130 pounds.

Explanation of the test automobile (A) The car model is (Ford AA) with a front and rear wheelbase of about 257 inches, a wheelbase of 62 inches, `S-AE` horsepower of 24.03 horsepower, 4 cylinders, a cylinder bore of 3 and 7/8 inches, a stroke of 4 and 1/4 inches, a load capacity of 1.5 tons, engine number `AA4062458`, tires front 2 rear 4` with dimensions of 6.00×20`, has traveled about 300 miles. (B) The body, iron frame and tarpaulin weigh 1,000 pounds. (C) Installation differences: No carburetor (Carburteer), replaced by a regulator. The original manual throttle lever has been changed to an air regulating lever. The foot-operated accelerator is connected to the tongue of the regulator. The generator and the first cleaner are placed side by side at the rear of the car body. The second cleaner is attached to the lower part of the rear of the frame.

Records before starting the car (A) Ignition: Total preparation time is 135 minutes. Gas is generated after 4.5 minutes of blowing, but the charcoal used is relatively wet and cannot be started. Blowing continues for 38.5 minutes before the engine is started. (B) Charcoal loading: Initially, 132 pounds of charcoal are loaded. After the engine is started, 34.7 pounds of charcoal are added. This charcoal is consumed by the ignition.

Records after starting the car (A) Route: From Changsha East Station to Xiangtan East Station, one way is 32.9 miles or 9.5 li, round trip is 65.8 miles or 183 li. The road surface is gravel road, and the terrain has a maximum slope of about 6%. (B) Passengers: 18 people on the way out, weighing 2270 pounds, 20 people on the way back, weighing 2520 pounds. (C) Time: 76 minutes and 30 seconds on the way out, 81 minutes and 30 seconds on the way back. The above time is the actual driving time, and all rest and charcoal adding time is excluded. (D) Charcoal adding: 29.2 pounds of charcoal were added at Yijiawan on the way out, taking 6 minutes including rest time, and 23.5 pounds of charcoal were added at Xiangtan, taking 68.5 minutes including rest time. (E) Remaining charcoal: 62 pounds of charcoal remained from Xiangtan back to Changsha. (F) Charcoal consumption: It takes 122.7 pounds of charcoal to travel 183 li, which is 0.67 pounds per li. If the charcoal consumed for ignition is included, the total consumption is 157.4 pounds, which is 0.86 pounds per li. (G) Parking: The first time I parked at Yijiawan for 6 minutes. I did not blow air when I started the car. The second time I parked at Xiangtan for 68.5 minutes. I blew air for 2 minutes when I restarted the car. (H) Speed: The maximum speed is 38 miles per hour, and the average speed is 25 miles per hour.

Testers (A) Representatives: Pi Zuoqiong, representative of the Central Ministry of Industry, and representatives from various provinces and circles, totaling 41 people. (B) Experts: Li Baohe, Mou Jiu, Zhang Zeng. (C) Construction Department Representatives: Xiang De, Liu Min. (October 20th)

Recent Status of Construction of Five Major Highways in Anhui 86

Jiang Telegraphed to Expedite Construction of the Wuhu-Tunxi Road

Wuhu-Zhapu Railway Actively Surveying

Wuhu Correspondence: In order to facilitate transportation in Anhui Province and meet the needs of military transport, the Anhui Provincial Government has formulated an overall plan to build five major highways: Jingwu (Nanjing to Wuhu), Wutun (Wuhu to Tunxi), Anhe (Anqing to Hefei), Anqiantai (Anqing to Qianshan Taihu), and Xiyu. Among them, the Anhe Road has already started construction or has been opened to traffic in advance, and the Jingwu Road is also being expedited within a time limit. This road is related to the transportation of Jiangsu and Anhui, and it can also connect the Shanghai-Hangzhou route, which is very important. Now 80 to 90% of the entire road project has been completed. Only the bridge project is still being carried out day and night. At the latest, it can be opened to traffic this year or next spring. As for the Wutun Highway, which goes directly from Wuhu to the inland areas of Tunxi and Huizhou, it is tantamount to opening the key to southern Anhui. Until today, those who enter Huizhou from various places still have to follow the land from Wuhu and use cars and sedan chairs instead of walking. Huizhou is mostly mountainous, and it often takes half a month to reach the top and bottom. Moreover, the area borders the Jiangxi border, which is very important for military operations to suppress bandits. Therefore, Chiang Kai-shek, commander-in-chief of bandit suppression in the three provinces, is extremely concerned about this line. Recently, he sent a special telegram to the Anhui Provincial Government, instructing Gao Tiejun, the chief county magistrate of Wuhu, to actively recruit workers during the slack season this winter, bring the previously issued survey charts, and go to supervise the construction in person, first dividing the earthwork into sections within a time limit, and limit him to quickly estimate and reply by telegram the unfinished earthwork and number of workers in the county of Wutun Road within three days. After receiving the order, Gao immediately agreed with the survey team and went to the forward to survey and estimate, so as to estimate and reply. At the same time, the Wuzha (Wuhu to Zhapu) light railway initiated by Zhang Jingjiang and others is now also setting up an office in Wu Zhai, Zaoshu Garden, Wuhu, with Chen Hong, two engineering experts, following the Xuanwuguang roadbed and actively surveying, hoping to complete it within two months, so that the bridges and tracks can be valued and handed over to the Shanghai road committee for design. It is said that the cost will be more than 20 million yuan. (October 21st)

Local Correspondence

Songjiang 87

County Magistrate Qian and Former Director of Hexiang Bureau Hold Final Accounts

The former director of the Hexiang Administrative Bureau, Zhang Yonglin, had advanced funds while in office, which was denied by the incumbent director, Zhu Guangxiong. The two sides argued and filed numerous official documents, and the case was suspended for several years after being ordered by the provincial department to be audited by the Songjiang County Government, but it has not been concluded. It is now known that the county government ordered the chief of the first district, Zhong Taishi, to invite Zhang Yonglin and Zhu Guangxiong to set a date for auditing, and informed both parties to reply. Subsequently, Zhang Yonglin replied by letter, stating that the other party had repeatedly broken his appointment for setting a date, and the auditing could not be completed. He sent a letter to Chief Zhong to forward it to the county government, requesting a date to be set to avoid the other party making excuses for postponing the meeting, and so on. It has recently been learned that the county government has notified former Director Zhu to set a date for auditing within five days and not to postpone it any further. At the same time, Chief Zhong was ordered to send a letter to both parties to urge them to complete the auditing within a time limit.

Inspection Tour of the Provincial Defense Committee Member in Songjiang 88

Qiu Mingjiu, an inspector from the Provincial Defense Committee, arrived in Songjiang two days ago to supervise and expedite the organization of the county's defense corps and to observe the conditions of the defense corps training class. Yesterday, he convened the second county defense committee meeting in the county government's conference hall. The meeting was presided over by Wang Zhewu, the vice chairman, and attended by Gu Yangtian, the head of the 16th district corps, and others. Qiu Mingjiu, from the Provincial Committee, reported on the significance the province attached to the defense corps, hoping that the county would complete its organization within the specified time. Wu Changding, director of the county defense committee's office, then reported on his trip to attend the Provincial Defense Committee meeting. Finally, the heads of each district exchanged opinions on the situation of compiling the "Jia" (first class) units as ordered, and then the meeting adjourned.

Kunshan: Major Fire in Zhongda Street 89

Zhongda Street in Kunshan is a prosperous commercial area. At 4:00 PM on the 21st, Zhang Daquan's foreign goods store accidentally caused a fire while repairing an air-pressure stove. The fire spread to the stored kerosene, making it uncontrollable. When the fire brigades from various districts heard the alarm, they rushed to the scene to put out the fire. However, the fire had already spread to the Zhu Xingtai tin foil shop across the street. Due to the large amount of Texaco kerosene stored in the shop, the fire intensified. It was not until 7:00 PM that the fire was extinguished. Several businesses were burned down, including Erxi Sanfang Bookstore, Bao Cheng Jewelry Store, and Yongli Shoe and Hat Store, with losses amounting to more than 100,000 yuan. When the fire broke out, a clerk from Zhang Daquan's store was burned and rescued by people. He was taken to Guangren Hospital for treatment. It is said that his injuries are serious and he may not survive.

Suzhou 90

Execution of Anhui Gang Leader by Firing Squad

Wu Xiaopangzi, also known as Hu Zhanghe, the leader of the Anhui gang, had been rampaging on Taihu Lake for eight years. On August 30th of this year, he was captured by Xu Pucheng, the first district chief of the water police, in Zhujing Town, which belongs to Jinshan County. He was then escorted to the Suzhou-Songjiang Water Bandit Suppression Headquarters, sentenced to death, and the sentence was submitted to the province for approval. Yesterday (the 22nd) at 2:00 PM, the prisoner was tied up and taken to Wangshudun execution ground outside the Guomen Gate and executed by firing squad.

Victims' Families from the City's West Side Appeal Against the Tragedy 91

The incident involving the shooting in the Shengjiabang area of Fulangzhong Lane, west of the city, due to a misunderstanding by the police about a robbery, has already been reported in this newspaper. Now, the families of the deceased, Chen Huasheng and Zhu Jinshu, have hired lawyer Wang Yunian to file a complaint with the District Prosecutor's Office, requesting that Fang Ziqing, the patrolman from the Fifth Precinct who first opened fire, be arrested and punished. Merchants from Taiping Bridge in Yangyu Lane and local people have initiated the organization of a relief association for the tragedy to handle the aftermath.

Wuxi: Extension of the Xicheng Highway Route 92

Since its completion, the Xicheng Highway has stretched for more than 90 li, connecting the traffic of the two counties and benefiting long-distance bus passengers. However, the northern section of the road only extended to the West Gate of Jiangyin and failed to reach the Jiangyin Pier. Therefore, the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Construction recently instructed the Jiangyin County Bureau of Construction to immediately extend the route to connect to the Yangtze River pier. After receiving the order, the bureau has dispatched personnel to survey the route, which is estimated to be about six li long. It is said that construction will begin soon.

Water Police Search for Lake Bandits 93

Recently, lake bandits have been rampant. Although the police team has fiercely suppressed them, they scatter and flee, making it difficult to eliminate them in one fell swoop. The day before yesterday, Zhang Guifang, the tenth team leader of the second district of the water police, was ordered to hire two lake boats at Xincunkou. He led 50 water police officers stationed in the mountains to Zhushan. They happened to meet Captain Sun of the ninth team, who also led 40 police officers on two lake boats to search various small mountains. Finding nothing, they patrolled the Jiaoshan and Tuoshan areas. The northwest wind picked up, and the large fishing boats all sailed to the South Lake. The bandit ships also took the opportunity to escape, resulting in no gains.

Changzhou: County Government Executes Three Bandits 94

The Wujin County Government previously apprehended Mo Debiao, Lou Zumao, Ji Shengda, and three other bandits who had committed robberies within the county. Upon interrogation, they confessed to committing serious crimes such as robbery without denying. They were sentenced to death and approved by the provincial government for execution. This morning (the 22nd) at 8:00 AM, the prisoners were brought to the scene, their identities were verified, and they were escorted to the execution ground and executed by firing squad.

Purchasing 10,000 Dan of Grain for Famine Relief 95

The Wujin Grain Management Committee held a meeting on the 21st and decided to temporarily withdraw savings to purchase 10,000 dan of new grain for famine relief. Huang Gongwang, Zhou Jiping, and Lin Junbao were publicly recommended to be responsible for the operation. In addition to the existing five warehouses, part of the Tianning Temple was borrowed for temporary storage.

Jiangyin: Merchants and Citizens Petition for Reduction of Defense Donation 96

Banditry is rampant in the area around Dongwai, the shoe shops, and Zhanwen Bridge. Magistrate Ma ordered Liu Youkang, the first district chief, to supervise the local merchants and wealthy individuals to establish a defense corps to maintain security. After receiving the order, Chief Liu went to the countryside and convened meetings with various merchants. After deliberation, it was decided to raise a large sum of money in the near future to purchase firearms. The merchants in the town, facing poor business conditions, found it difficult to bear the burden of the allocation. On the 20th, they sent representatives to petition Magistrate Ma, requesting a reduction in the burden and leniency towards the merchants.

Capture of the Chief Culprit in the Chenzhangba Robbery Case 97

Wang Xiao Da's family in Chenzhangba, Zhanwen Bridge, Dongwai, was robbed by bandits the day before yesterday, and the entire family was burned down, including an 85-year-old mother who was burned to death. After this case occurred, Magistrate Ma immediately ordered the district to cooperate in arresting the bandits. The day before yesterday (the 20th), the 2nd District Defense Corps captured Fei Jifu in Feijia Village. Fei confessed to accomplices including Wan Shengbao, Wan Genshi, Ma Lincai, and Ma Qingtang, who were subsequently arrested. Yesterday morning (the 21st), the ringleader, Qin Ganquan, was captured in the city. In the afternoon, all of them were taken to the county for interrogation.

Zhenjiang 98

Bureau of Education Distributes School Funds

The County Bureau of Education, faced with the difficulty of maintaining operations due to the failure to receive school funds for the schools and social education institutions under its jurisdiction for several months, has sought various means and has raised funds for the June and July school payments. All schools etc. have been notified to bring their credentials to the bureau on October 24th to receive payment.

Theft Occurs in the Seventh District 99

Thirty or so bandits armed with box cannons came to Xinba Town, Kunlian, in the seventh district of the county yesterday, and robbed Wang Futai Rice Shop and Wantai Grocery Store. By the time the defense corps from Laoba Town and other places heard the news and rushed to the scene, the bandits were gone.

Danyang: Two Reactionary Criminals Escorted to the Province for Interrogation 100

Zhu Di and Zhu Fuqing, father and son, from Zhujia Village in the tenth district of the northern countryside, were secretly reported to the province for a case. The provincial government specifically ordered the county to secretly arrest and investigate. Magistrate Wang followed the order and sent police officers to arrest Zhu Di and his son on the spot and searched out many letters. They have now been sent to the province. Also, Tang Laosi, a resident of Houqiu Village in the western countryside, was suspected of being a communist. He was reported by the county and arrested by the county government and was also escorted to the Provincial Provisional Military Tribunal for interrogation yesterday.

Yangzhou: Another Wave of Tax Collection Unrest in the Second District 101

Tax collection unrest erupted again in the Second District of Jiangdu on the morning of the 21st. At that time, gongs sounded everywhere, and many women and children, holding farm tools, gathered at the gap in Xu Ningmen, at the ferry crossing outside the Dongguan City gate on the opposite bank of the river, preventing vegetable and manure carriers from entering the city. They also smashed manure buckets and dumped manure and vegetables into the river. The provincial security team came to stop them, but they refused to obey, and 47 people, including Xia Widow, were arrested. Subsequently, the county magistrate led two teams of detectives and police officers out of the city to escort them into the city. Yang Juansheng, the deputy chief of the police team, interrogated them one by one, and they all claimed that they were not organized but were arrested while passing by. Zang Liuqi, the chief of the second district, has gone to the county to bail them out and learned that the county magistrate has scheduled a meeting with the township chiefs of the second district at the tax collection office in the Taiyang Palace on the 23rd to find ways to guide them to avoid further complications.

Ten Bandits Escorted to the Security Office for Interrogation 102

A bandit den was discovered in Erli Bridge, outside Dongguan, in the county. When the detective team went to arrest them, they were shot at by the bandits, and an investigator, Sun Jintang, was killed on the spot. Five bandits, including Jiang Guohong, were arrested. They have now been interrogated by the county and confessed to robbing Yuan Zhenggui of Huaiziqiao in the northern countryside and others. On the 21st, they submitted a confession along with the five bandits, including Jiang, to the Security Office for interrogation. It is also learned that Zhu Guoan, Chen Ruizhi, Chen Ruisheng, Dai Jinfu, and Sun Changlin, who were arrested in connection with the cases of robbing firearms from the Qishumiao police defense post and intercepting ships and extorting tickets from the Xinghua gang, were also submitted to the office for legal handling at the same time.

Nantong: Jiangbei Bandit Leader Attempts to Escape from Prison 103

Feng Ziyun, a Jiangbei bandit leader, was arrested in Liuqiao by the police team and sent to the county government for interrogation. While under investigation, Feng bribed a fellow prisoner in jail. On the 21st, he used a hacksaw to cut off his shackles and attempted to escape. However, the guards discovered the attempt and found the hacksaw and more than two hundred yuan of silver in the cell. After reporting to the county for interrogation, he was shackled with double shackles.

Jiang Chao Xiong's Missing Weapons and Ammunition Have Been Verified 104

Jiang Chao Xiong, the fourth district chief of the Jiangsu Maritime Public Security, was dismissed from his post by the Department of Civil Affairs for investigation after losing a large quantity of firearms and ammunition. He is now being held at the Provincial Public Security Bureau. The lost weapons and ammunition have now been verified by the new district chief, Zhang Xianyi, to include 48 rifles, 6 carbines, 28 discarded gun barrels, 2 old rifles, 21 bayonets for Type 79 rifles, 962 barrels of local gunpowder, 31 pounds and 6 ounces of foreign gunpowder, half a barrel of smokeless powder, 476 2.7-inch artillery shells, and 389 2.7-inch quick-firing gun fuses. These items could not be carried out due to the outbreak of the Shanghai War. However, one Type 79 rifle, two Browning pistols, 2,325 rounds of 9mm rifle ammunition, 2,694 rounds of Type 79 rifle ammunition, 1,802 rounds of Mauser pistol ammunition, and 4,102 rounds of hand-held machine gun ammunition have not been handed over. The situation was submitted to the province for approval on the 21st.

Jiaxing 105

Patrol Officer Privately Releases Opium Offender, Subject to Investigation

Sheng A-quan and Sheng Changhong, who run a teahouse, and Jin Zhitang, a storyteller at the teahouse, were found to be privately smoking opium in Shengjialang Xiatang in the northern countryside of Jiaxing. The news was reported to the Langxia Police Station, and Patrol Officer Dai Boshu immediately ordered Police Chief Li Yaoting, Patrol Officer Li Jinsheng, and Xu Changde to search the premises. Thirteen sets of opium smoking paraphernalia were found, and Sheng A-quan, Sheng Changhong, and Jin Zhitang were arrested. After a brief interrogation by Patrol Officer Dai, they were detained. That night, Sheng Xin-yi, the village chief of Meihu Township, and several teachers from Meihu Elementary School went to intercede. After several discussions with Patrol Officer Dai, the suspects were not released. The next day, they hired a boat to escort the opium offenders to the Wangjiangjing Third Sub-bureau. When the boat reached the north gate of Wangjiangjing, a small boat suddenly approached and swapped Ru Jinsheng, a beggar on the small boat, with Sheng A-quan from Patrol Officer Dai's boat. When the case was brought to the sub-bureau, Chief Ting Zhichun asked questions and found suspicious points. He then strictly investigated the matter and found out the truth. He asked the county bureau chief for instructions and was ordered to send the patrol officer to Jiaxing for investigation. On the 21st, the sub-bureau chief sent Patrol Officer Dai and the opium offenders to the county bureau, which in turn sent them to the court for investigation.

Letter

Letter from Datong Oil, Sugar and Paper Industry Association 107

To the Editor: After reviewing the "Important News" column on page 2 of your newspaper on October 17, we found the statement "60-70% of the shops were burned" in the report "Two Disasters in Datong". This is inconsistent with the facts. Here is a brief account of the actual fire incident on that day. At 10:30 PM on the 13th of this month, a thatched house belonging to the Jiang family on the Hengdi in Zhoutou caught fire due to carelessness. At that time, the southeast wind was very strong, and hundreds of thatched houses on the embankment were burned down. Then, the wind suddenly turned northeast, causing the thatched houses outside the embankment along the river to be burned as well. Before long, the wind changed to due east and then burned westward, burning down about 800 houses, covering an area of about 300 mu. There were about 4,000 disaster victims, all of whom were laborers. It was an unprecedented disaster, too tragic to bear. Fortunately, it was still far from the city of Datong, and no shops were burned. In accordance with the facts, we hereby send this letter with the hope that your newspaper will investigate and promptly correct the error, and we will be very grateful. Wang Daolong, Chairman of the Datong Oil, Sugar and Paper Industry Association, October 20.

Page 11

Educational News (Special Report)

Preliminary Suggestions for Reforming Chinese School Education 108

(12) Cheng Tianfang

How should a political university be run? Absolutely not many political universities should be set up. One or two in the whole country is enough. The political university should have internal affairs, finance, transportation, justice, education, police administration, land, surveying and other subjects. High school graduates should be enrolled and given five years of training. The political university should focus on academic research on the one hand, and pay special attention to the cultivation of personality, the practice of group life, and the development of management ability on the other. Nowadays, people engaged in politics in China have too strong a sense of selfishness and too weak a sense of responsibility. Therefore, the phenomena of greed, corruption, procrastination, perfunctoriness, infighting, and exclusion are fully exposed in the political arena. How can politics not be corrupt and the country not be refined? If we want to reform politics, we must first change the atmosphere. If we want to change the atmosphere, we must first cultivate talents who can change the atmosphere. This mission is what the political university should shoulder. Therefore, the political university should pay special attention to cultivating students' brave, sacrificial, honest, and pure character, orderly and methodical management ability, harmonious cooperation, and spirit of solidarity in abiding by the law and obeying public opinion. Anyone who shows shortcomings in these areas, even if their academic performance is excellent, will have to be reluctantly let go.

All expenses of political university students while they are in school are provided by the government, but after graduation, their intelligence and ability should be completely dedicated to the country and be subject to the country's command. The government should consider the subjects they have studied and the nature of their skills, and assign them to serve in local or central government agencies. Initially, they should all be given the title of trainee and paid the minimum salary. After the training period expires, they should be promoted level by level according to their performance. After a considerable period of assessment, if they are indeed capable, have an upright character, and are not affected by customs and able to change the atmosphere, then they should be given heavy responsibilities, such as county magistrate. Of course, even if the political university implements extremely strict training, no one can guarantee that everyone who comes out of it will become a political talent. However, assuming that several hundred students graduate from the political university every year, and after training, dozens of them become good county magistrates, and dozens of them become good secretaries and section chiefs (as long as it is done well, this is probably not difficult), then after ten or twenty years, the political atmosphere will surely change, and the goal of reforming politics will not be difficult to achieve, and the political university will have fulfilled its purpose.

Since political universities are established separately, the political and legal departments of other national universities can be merged into the political university. As for private universities, they can be allowed to train professional talents such as lawyers and accountants to serve the society, but the important task of cultivating political leaders cannot be placed in their hands. Some people may say that Chinese people have always had a particularly strong desire to become officials, so there are particularly many and well-developed private law schools and political science schools. If the state runs a political university and guarantees employment after graduation, wouldn't it further promote the idea of becoming an official? I think it is still true that Chinese people have a strong desire to become officials, but there are other reasons for the large number of private law schools and political science schools and the high number of students. First, law departments are easy to run, unlike engineering, agriculture, science, etc., which require large amounts of equipment costs, so private schools mostly run law departments. Second, private schools mostly accept all students who come, so students who originally did not want to enter law departments can only enter private law schools or political science schools because they cannot get into other schools. We only need to look at the fact that only 114 people applied for the political science department of National Zhejiang University this year, while about 200 people applied for the electrical engineering department, to see that most high school graduates do not want to study political science anymore. As for the reason why the idea of becoming an official is so strong, it is because the power of officials is too great, which attracts a group of people to envy them. If the government reduces the power of officials and increases their responsibilities, the concept can be changed immediately. For example, although students of the political university receive special treatment from the government while they are in school and are employed by the government after graduation, it seems like special preferential treatment, but their freedom is dedicated to the country. They cannot refuse if the government sends them to serve in remote provinces or poor areas, and they cannot refuse if the government gives them the minimum salary. On the other hand, if an engineering university graduate has strong ability and good opportunities, he may be able to earn a salary of more than 100 yuan immediately after graduation. In terms of personal life, he is much freer and more comfortable than a political university graduate. Therefore, in this way, people who do not have a particularly strong sense of service and a strong sense of responsibility may not want to enter the political university, so how can it promote the idea of becoming an official?

Inauguration Ceremony of Directors and Supervisors of the Municipal Board of Education Held 110

The directors and supervisors of this year's Board of Education have been legally elected and have convened a meeting. The details have been reported in the previous newspaper. Yesterday morning at 9:00 AM, the inauguration ceremony was held at the Bureau of Education. The details are listed below:

Agenda: (1) Ringing the bell to open the meeting, (2) Standing up in unison, (3) Singing the Party song, (4) Paying the highest tribute to the Party and national flag and the portrait of the President, (5) The chairman respectfully reads the President's will, (6) Chairman's report, (7) Speech by the supervisor, (8) Directors and supervisors take oath, (9) Speeches by guests, (10) Response speeches, (11) Taking photos, (12) Ceremony concludes and meeting adjourns.

Attendees: (1) Directors and supervisors Tao Baichuan, Zhou Feicheng, Xu Zeyu, Zhang Zhongdao, Huang Zaoxiong, Chen Bai, Zheng Tan, Wang Dechang, Wu Renqi, Zhang Xiaotian, Zhang Yousan, Wu Xiu, Zhou Darong, Zheng Hongnian, Du [blank], Zhang Zaibo, Ma Jiazhen, Cheng Kuanzheng, Wang Yongzhi, Chen Jicheng, Yang Jingyi, Hao Naiding, Gu Yinqian, Wu Kaixian, Mao Yun, (2) Supervisors Zhou [blank] Ze, representative of the Municipal Party Headquarters, Zeng Shengdian, representative of the Municipal Government, (3) Guests Jin Ke [blank] of the Land Bureau, Wang Qin of Jinan University, Wu Rugui of the Ninth District Party Headquarters, Hu Wenyao of Aurora University, and more than 100 other people.

Summary of Speeches: (1) Chairman Zhang Zhongdao reported that the city occupies a very important position in the country due to the development of industry and commerce and the large population. Therefore, the city's education should be actively expanded to meet the needs of the environment, especially paying attention to the development of social education in addition to school education. The colleagues of this association will contribute all their energy and experience to the educational administrative organs, in order to expect the development of the city's entire education. (2) Zhou Lianze, representative of the Municipal Party Headquarters, said that education is a kind of political facility. Our Party takes the Three Principles of the People as the guiding principle for saving the country. Therefore, all educational facilities should be carried out in accordance with the spirit of the Three Principles of the People. I hope that all the colleagues of the Municipal Education Association can uphold this essential meaning and help promote the development of the city's education. (3) Zeng Shengdian, representative of the Mayor, said that the board of directors and supervisors produced by the Municipal Education Association is the crystallization of talents from elementary, middle and high schools in the city. In the future, it will surely provide great help to the city's educational administrative agencies. However, I believe that the decline of China's national fortune today is due to the decline of production undertakings. Therefore, I very much hope that you will devote yourself to the research of production education, so that production undertakings can be developed. Wang Jichuan and other guests also gave speeches, and the length of the speeches is omitted. Finally, Zheng Hongnian, a representative of the directors and supervisors, gave a speech on behalf of all the directors and supervisors. The meeting adjourned.

Westerners' Club Group A Match 115

Donghua Overcomes French Business

Chen Jiaqiu and Li Yichen Each Score a Goal

The French Business Team Put On a Wonderful Performance

Separated for three days, one must look at them with new eyes. Yesterday's wonderful performance by the French Business team on the baseball field was truly astonishing. Fortunately, Donghua had the defense of a golden city and iron wall, and the sharp and agile warriors in attack, and finally won two goals from the strong and capable opponents, and returned in triumph.

No Way for Heroes to Approach the Goal

For a time, it was rumored that the famous Scottish referee Davidson was officiating his first match in Shanghai in the Donghua vs. French Business game yesterday. At the sound of three whistles, the battle began. Donghua seized the initiative, dividing its forces to attack. Wan Xianghua stood up, and the ball moved from the left to the center, turning into a corner kick. Wu Youliang saw the opportunity and shot, from more than twenty yards away, hitting the upper goalpost and bouncing backward. Chen Yutian received the ball and moved from the right to the center, shooting at the goal. The shot was blocked. For a time, the brave generals surrounded the enemy's goal, each displaying their skills. The enemy's pillar, Ma Er, strong and powerful, snatched the ball and escaped danger.

One Goal Shakes All in Attendance

The French Business wave had just passed, and they led the crowd to invade. Feng Tu and Wu resisted in front, and Li Guan assisted behind. Zhou Xianyan had no chance to be a hero. At twenty-five minutes, Donghua increased the pressure, turning into a corner kick. Wan Xianghua passed the ball well, and Li Yichen rushed in fiercely. The goalkeeper was startled. Chen Jiaqiu landed a kick, breaking the goal. As soon as one goal was scored, all in attendance were greatly shaken.

The Enemy General Labors in Vain

French Business, losing a goal, was not discouraged at all. They still advanced whenever they had the opportunity, entering every space. However, their skills were lacking, and their luck was not good. Until the first half, they were at a disadvantage with a score of zero to one. In the second half, their spirits were uplifted, and they fought hard. The three players in the center were particularly good, and the two wings were still acceptable, but the entire line could not form a cohesive whole and use each other. Therefore, in extremely good situations, Donghua was always seen breaking through the encirclement and escaping danger, unable to achieve its ultimate goal, which was due to each acting on their own. About ten minutes later, Fa Fanqie of Right Wing almost scored a goal, but his forearm touched the ball before kicking it, so it was invalid even though it went in. He labored in vain.

The Header Skill is Amazing

After this, Donghua encountered a second danger. French Business had the opportunity to take a free kick, which was just outside the penalty area. Inner defender Marseille, at the request of the whole team, personally stepped forward. Fa Fanqie missed the direction, but it was seized by Donghua. The crowd was pleased, but due to a miscommunication of the signal, they gained nothing. Instead, Wan hooked the ball from the baseline, and Chen Jiaqiu rushed up with a kick but missed. Wan passed it again, and Chen Hongguang followed closely. The defender left the goal to make an emergency save. The ball suddenly veered to the right. Chen Yutian saw it, and the ball was falling right in front of him. He rushed forward, but suddenly a rescuer came diagonally, and Chen was blocked by him, unable to fulfill his ambition. After that, Chen kicked a corner kick, which was perfectly placed. Li Yichen jumped out of the crowd and headed the ball in. With two goals already scored, the situation was set. Donghua, in a balanced situation, shifted and took the upper hand. The forwards continued to press, gaining a great advantage. French Business resisted with all their might, and nothing happened. They hit the goalpost twice, which should be considered fortunate. Finally, Zhou Xianyan caught Fa Fanqie's ball in the air, which was greatly praised by the whole field. In the end, Donghua won 2-0.

Inter-Port Tennis, Day One 116

Shanghai Team Has the Advantage

Singles: Zheng Jia Zhao Defeats Fen Qiao

Doubles: Hui Ka vs. Luo Brothers Tie

Hong Kong, 22nd - Today was the first day of the Shanghai-Hong Kong Inter-Port Tennis Tournament. The weather was very good, with a slight breeze. As a result, Shanghai won the first point. In singles, Zheng Jia Zhao, a rising young player from Shanghai, defeated Fen Qiao, a strong player from Hong Kong, 2-6, 6-3, 6-4, 3-6, 6-1. In doubles, Hui Te, Kanavalo, and the Luo Wenhui brothers from Hong Kong each won two sets. It was getting dark, and the match will continue at 10 a.m. tomorrow. The result was 6-4, 5-7, 3-6, 6-4.

The Singles Match 117

Zheng Zhao Jia (Shanghai) (2-6, 6-3, 6-4, 3-6, 6-1) Fen Qiao (Hong Kong)

Both sides appeared nervous at the start, but Fen Qiao gradually calmed down, while Zheng made repeated serving errors. Fen Qiao won the first set 6-2. In the second set, Fen took a 3-0 lead, winning with an overhead smash. But Zheng then showed his real skill, winning six consecutive games. In the third set, Fen again took a 4-2 lead, but Zheng won four consecutive games. In the fourth set, Zheng took a 2-0 lead, approaching the net to volley, but Fen shot to his left and right, winning 6-3 to tie the sets at 2-2. In the final set, Fen Qiao was completely defeated and could not recover, with wild shots all over the court. Zheng won a big victory 6-1.

The Doubles Match 118

Hui Te Kanavalo (Shanghai) (6-4, 5-7, 3-6, 6-4) Luo Wenhui Brothers (Hong Kong)

The Shanghai team started smoothly, with Hui Te's serve and smash overwhelming the Luo Wenhui brothers. The two Luo's usual cooperation completely fell apart. The Shanghai team won the first set 6-4. The second set was fiercely contested. The Shanghai team took a 2-0 lead, but due to overconfidence and carelessness, they lost 5-7. In the third set, the two Luo brothers launched a perfect coordinated attack, with many long rallies and equal scores. The two Luos won again 6-3. In the fourth set, both sides played very well, but Kanavalo made many errors, and Hui Te was too eager to win, gradually showing fatigue. As a result, Shanghai won 6-4. The decisive fifth set will be played at 10 a.m. tomorrow.

Central Youth Women's Volleyball Finals 119

Wuben Wins the Championship

3-1 Overwhelms Haixing

The Skills are Truly Worthy of Praise

Yesterday, the Wuben Women's Volleyball Team, with their exquisite skills, once again overwhelmed their strong opponent, the Haixing Team, to win the championship of the Central Youth First Women's Volleyball League. The result was 3-1, with scores of 21-12, 21-17, 24-26, 21-12.

Wuben is Ineffable Wuben's volleyball skills are superb and flawless. The sophistication of their cooperation and the smoothness of their coordination are beyond description; one can only call it ineffable. The talent is balanced, and each player excels in their role. The spikes of Zhang, Li, and Wang in the front row are capable of surprise attacks, catching people off guard, especially Zhang Biru's ruthless methods, which leave people helpless. Xue Zhijie, sitting in the center, is highly skilled and hardworking in setting up the ball from the back row. The championship is well-deserved.

Haixing is Slightly Inferior In terms of individual technique, Haixing is definitely not inferior to Wuben. The reason for their loss is poor coordination and uneven talent. The fierce players are a cut above, while the weak players are too weak. The talent is scattered, and there is no way to train together. The most outstanding players on the team are Wang Chunruo, Su Zuqi, and Huang Xingfen, followed by Guan Liuzhu. The rest make frequent errors, and their positions are disorganized. The back row moves too far forward, sometimes squeezing each other, which Wuben took advantage of. It's a pity.

Two Consecutive Sets In the first attack, Haixing was frustrated by Wuben 5-1. Wuben chased closely, and the score was very close, 5-5, and then Wuben won the half-set first at 11-9. Xue Zhijie added four points in a row, and the situation changed. 15-9, 18-11. Li Po made it 21-12, and Wuben won the first set. In the second set, Haixing still found it difficult to develop, and again lost the half-set first at 7-11, falling behind 16-9. At this time, Huang Xingfen suddenly added three points, giving Haixing hope of a turnaround. But at this time, Xue Zhijie made repeated mistakes, and Haixing was only two points behind at 17-19. Unfortunately, Wuben still won this second set 21-17.

Haixing Begins to Fight Hard Under adverse circumstances, Haixing began to fight hard. In the third set, Haixing, although trailing by two points at 3-5, Su Zuqi added three points in a row to lead 6-5. Wang Xiangying also led 10-9. Unexpectedly, in this good opportunity, Xingfen and Zuzhen collided. Next, Wuben, after a kill by Li Po, still won the half-set first at 11-10. The scores of the two teams after that were sometimes only one point apart, difficult to resolve, and the whole audience was tense. Wuben won a point at 20-19, and after a kill by Su Zuqi, it was equal again. After each scoring 24 points, Haixing took a gamble and won back the third set 26-24.

Wuben Wins the Championship Haixing won back one set, posing a great threat to Wuben. Sure enough, 6-3, 9-6, 10-9, victory after victory. Unexpectedly, when it was Wuben's turn to serve, Zhang Jia Sui scored seven points in a row, which became a fatal blow to Haixing. 17-12. Finally, in the fourth set at 21-12, Wuben won a total of 3-1. The warriors of the two teams are as follows:

New Basketball Techniques (17) (Not to Be Reprinted) Original by Claire Burcky, Translated by Zhang Guoxun and Qian Yiqin 122

To apply this formation, there must be a tall center and three agile teammates, and they must all be able to catch the ball steadily, so that the game can be played smoothly and cooperatively. This method is commonly seen in the American [Ten University Games]. Number four pretends to rush to the free throw line, then turns to the right of his opponent's guard and passes the ball to number two, who is rushing out of the corner. After receiving the ball, number two dribbles into the arc of the free throw area. At this time, number two's guard is temporarily blocked by number four. The tall center, number one, should rush out of the corner and catch number two's pass at the free throw line. After catching the ball, he (number one) turns slightly and passes it back to number two. At this time, number three has run straight to the basket along the sideline. Number two then passes the ball to him (number three) to let him shoot.

American Cotton Slightly Declines Last Week 132

丨Southern Hedging Sales Are Very Active丨

A telegram from New York on the 21st reports on the cotton market during the week, stating that an increase in hedging sales led to buying by traders, but only when prices fell. As a result, the cotton market slightly declined last week. Most of the transactions were limited by domestic political situation and waiting for the development of the spot market. The Southern hoarding movement continues, and some people want to replenish their October futures contracts, so they have to pay the highest basis price of the season. The market changes are due to reorganization, and the difference between the market prices in New York and Liverpool is used to maintain the fluctuations of the gold pound exchange rate. Cotton production is extremely difficult to estimate, although some believe that production will be revised downwards. The amount of hedging sales and its attraction are currently valued by people.
