Grains Rice Market Eases by Five to Six Cents 135

Hunan There are more than 150 rice boats in the pond, so the arrival of goods has been limited recently. Today, counterparts from Wujiang Tongli and other places came to Shanghai to meet with the leaders of the Shanghai firms and invited the municipal government, the Social Affairs Bureau, and the Chamber of Commerce to mediate satisfactorily. As a result, the situation has eased, and wild rice and white rice have fallen sharply by five to six cents. Xixin japonica rice has also followed by a small two or three cents. Kiln-grown Baige Duyangjian has each fallen by two cents.

Xinzha Today, more than 40 ships arrived, and the situation has been on a downward spiral. The transactions between urban and rural stores and merchants are quite small. The opening prices of japonica rice from Kunshan, Yixing, Suzhou, and other places have each fallen by three to four cents. Kiln-grown Baige has fallen by a short two or three cents. The Changxi merchants are neither happy nor sad in the market.

Flour Market Greatly Weakened in the Afternoon 136

Yesterday, after the flour market opened in the morning, the prices of each month were generally stable. Because the quotation of foreign wheat improved by about 10 cents, most of the large and small factories waited and watched, and there were not many transactions. People's minds gradually stabilized, and the distant months seemed to be 0.5 to 0.75 cents better than the previous day. When it opened in the afternoon, it was initially stable, but then it fell again, because it was rumored that the pricing of Australian wheat was also cheap, only 3.6 taels, and Japanese merchants were directly dumping foreign flour to Tianjin, it was heard that it was only 1.7 taels. The Yufeng was also dumping in the distant months, so people's minds were greatly weakened, and prices fell step by step. Seeing the step-by-step pressure of foreign flour and wheat, even the prediction that the flour price would reach 1.75 taels in the future is probably still questionable. As a result, this month fell by 0.75 cents compared with the previous day, November and December fell by 1.2 cents, January fell by 1 cent, and February and March fell by 0.5 cents.

Wheat Futures Resist Short Selling and Tend to Strengthen 137

Yesterday, the wheat futures market was very quiet after the opening in the morning. Because the quotation of foreign wheat slightly improved by about 10 cents, there were few sellers, and the bulls did not dare to take action, resulting in very few transactions. There was little short selling. When it opened in the afternoon, the transaction was slightly more lively, and the market atmosphere also showed a slight strengthening. After the big drop the day before, there were not many people who released real chips, so some short sellers covered their positions, and people's minds seemed to be stable. However, at this time when foreign wheat is becoming increasingly loose, there is little hope for the future. As a result, this month and February each improved by 1 cent, March improved by 2 cents, and February was unchanged. The spot wheat did not open all day due to the quiet arrival and sales.

Silk and Tea New York Chinese Silk Sales Increase Sharply 140

The amount of silk consumed last month was 2,634 bales.

The previous month was only 856 bales, an increase of more than 1,000 bales.

New York silk mills, in view of the fact that Japanese silk prices are cheap but the quality is poor, and cannot be woven into silk alone, must be combined with Chinese silk, so the sales of Chinese silk have increased sharply. Last month (i.e., September), a total of 2,634 bales of white, yellow, gray, and Cantonese silk were consumed by the mills. The previous month (i.e., August) was only 856 bales, an increase of more than 1,700 bales.

Hardware British Steel Plates Rise Step by Step 142

The British steel plate market standard was declining day by day due to large inventories and few outlets. Looking at all aspects of the environment, there was almost an unmanageable situation. Therefore, the industry was hesitant to order goods. Therefore, there have been no goods arriving in the market for several months. Although the transaction has not been very prosperous in the past few days, it has been much more active than before. Therefore, the market goods are inevitably in short supply, and the standard has a step-by-step upward trend. The main ones are listed below.

2.5 Cents Stockpiles Deep, Transaction Slight This cargo has a slightly larger inventory, but the outlet has seemed thin in recent days. Therefore, the market price is not as strong as 5 cents, etc. It is estimated that the price is 7 taels and 7 mace and 5 cents per dan. It is heard that only sixty or seventy dans have been offered. The importer is from the Changjiang gang.

5 Cents Spot Goods Thin, Customer Sales Strong Customer transactions have a lot of decoration for 5 cents of color. In the past few days, 4-500 dans have been offered. The price is 6 taels, which is 2 mace and 5 cents better than before. However, looking at the thinness of the arrival of goods and the firmness of people's minds, the future market is very promising.

7.5 Cents Qingdao Sales Lead The Qingdao gang is very serious about the 7.5-cent business, so in the past few days, they have also sold 600 pieces. The price is 5 taels and 7 mace and 5 cents, which is also 2 mace and 5 cents higher than before. However, the business in this street is also good recently, and the market goods are in short supply. The standard has a hope of improving again.

1 Cent Business is Best in This Street The shipyards and machinery factories in this street have a strong appetite for the 1 cent color. Export business seems to be limited, and the market price is very firm. It is estimated to be 5 taels and 2 mace and 5 cents.

Wang Jingwei Left the Country Yesterday 143

The heads of all ministries went to see him off.

Mr. Wang is thin but in good spirits.

Dr. Noel's whole family accompanied him for care.

Wang Jingwei, the President of the Executive Yuan, left Shanghai on the French mail ship Andre Lebon at 11 o'clock yesterday morning to recuperate in Germany. Those who accompanied him were Wang's wife, Ms. Chen Bijun, Wang's two daughters, and secretaries Li Haoju, Chen Yuan, and Chen Da. Zeng Zhongming, the Vice Minister of the Railway Department, escorted him to Hong Kong and then returned to Shanghai. The heads of all ministries of the Executive Yuan and Wang's relatives and friends all went to the pier to see him off. The details are recorded below.

The Grand Occasion of the Farewell 144

From 8:00 AM to 10:00 AM yesterday morning, those who boarded the ship one after another to see him off included Acting President of the Executive Yuan and Minister of Finance Song Ziwen, Minister of Military Affairs He Yingqin, Minister of the Navy Chen Shaokuan, Minister of Foreign Affairs Luo Wengan, Chief of Staff Zhu Peide, Minister of Industry Chen Gongbo, Minister of Railways Gu Mengyu, Minister of Education Zhu Jiahua, Chairman of the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission Shi Qingyang, Director of the National Health Administration Liu Ruiheng, Vice Minister of Foreign Affairs Liu Chongjie, Vice Minister of the Interior Peng Xuepei, Central Committee member Ye Chucang, Secretary of the Central Political Council Tang Youren, Secretary of the Executive Yuan Chu Minyi and his wife, and Chiang Kai-shek's representative Zhang Qun, Yan Xishan's representative Zhao Pilian, Shanghai Mayor Wu Tiecheng, Jianghai Customs Superintendent Tang An, former Minister of Foreign Affairs Wang Zhengting, Municipal Public Security Bureau Director Wen Hongen, French Consul in Shanghai Mei Liai, and dozens of Wang's relatives and friends. The central dignitaries gathered at the port, which was quite a grand occasion.

The Situation of Boarding the Ship 145

The French mail ship was docked at the China Merchants Bureau Middle Wharf in Outer Hongqiao. After 8:00 AM, dozens of people, including those who were seeing off Mr. Wang Jingwei and those who were sending him off, took photos on the ship (taken by Li Zunyong).

And reporters from various newspapers arrived one after another. They waited until 10:30, but Mr. Wang had not yet arrived. Just as they were anxious, unexpectedly, in order to avoid the noise and for the sake of careful vigilance, Mr. Wang secretly changed to the Jinghui launch of the Customs at the Xinguang Wharf and boarded the ship from the outer barrier. In advance, Wen Hongen, the Director of the Public Security Bureau, led the police to guard the Xinguang Wharf. Song Ziwen, Zhu Peide, and Chen Shaokuan arrived first. At about 10 o'clock, Mr. and Mrs. Wang and their daughters arrived and took the Jinghui launch together to the side of the French ship. At 10:20, Mr. Wang and his party boarded the ship and went to the first-class cabin to rest.

Wang's Face is Thin 146

When President Wang boarded the ship, the people who were seeing him off were chatting in the corridor outside the cabin. When they heard that Mr. Wang had arrived, they rushed to the reception room. The reporters who were waiting at the port also rushed to board. The reception room was narrow and crowded. Mr. Wang sat alone at the head of the case, resting slightly. Then he stood up, put his left hand on the table, raised his right hand and shook hands with the send-off one by one to greet him. After the handshake, the crowd stood around and chatted. Mr. Wang wore a moss green robe, talked and laughed with the guests, and was in good spirits, but his face was thinner than before, and he often stroked his waist with his right hand, as if he was very uncomfortable. Gu Mengyu saw this and asked if he was comfortable. Mr. Wang politely replied that he had talked for too long yesterday (i.e., the day before), and today (i.e., yesterday) he had to travel by boat, so he felt slightly uncomfortable. He thought he could gradually recover after resting in the ship for a few days.

Talk to Reporters 147

The reporters from various newspapers then had a two-minute conversation with Mr. Wang. According to Mr. Wang, he was suffering from tropical diseases and wanted to recover quickly, so he went abroad for treatment. There are no specialized hospitals for treating tropical diseases in England, France, and Germany, so which country to go to for treatment will be decided after landing in Marseille. He could not predict when he would return to China. He had to wait for the doctor's diagnosis before he could be sure. The opening date of the Third Plenary Session of the Central Committee was imminent, and he was afraid that he would not be able to make it in time. He would entrust someone to submit his proposal at that time.

Set Sail at Eleven O'Clock 148

At 10:40, the guests who were seeing off said goodbye to Mr. Wang one after another. The reporters obtained Mr. Wang's consent and invited him to the deck to take pictures, while Mrs. Chen Bijun and her daughters stayed in a corner of the room, chatting with Mrs. Chen's mother and female relatives, unable to bear to part. It was not until the guest bell rang that they said goodbye to each other and went down the ship one after another. At 11:10, with a whistle, the wheel drums left the port.

Wu Tiecheng Hosted a Banquet 149

After the dignitaries said goodbye to President Wang, Shanghai Mayor Wu Tiecheng hosted a banquet at Xinghualou on Fourth Road at noon yesterday, and invited business leaders such as Qia Qing, Wang Xiaolai, and Qin Runqing to accompany him. The banquet was a great success. It was not until 2 o'clock that it broke up.

Noel's Statement 150

Mr. Wang invited German doctor Noel to accompany him to Germany this time in order to examine his condition, take care of the medication, and monitor his vision along the way. Dr. Noel's wife and son originally wanted to return home, but Mr. Wang asked them to travel together. They all left on the French mail ship Andre Lebon yesterday morning. According to Dr. Noel, once Mr. Wang's illness is cured, he will return to Shanghai at any time. The period is expected to be in early spring next year. During the period of his departure from Shanghai, the diagnosis and treatment of the Noel Hospital in this port will be temporarily presided over by two assistants.

Dignitaries Return to Beijing 151

Minister of Military Affairs He Yingqin, Chief of Staff Zhu Peide, Minister of the Navy Chen Shaokuan, Vice Minister of Foreign Affairs Liu Chongjie, Central Committee member Bai Yunti, Zhao Pilian, and Song Ziliang all took the night train to Beijing last night. Luo Wengan and Chen Gongbo will take the special express train to Beijing this morning.

Take the Queen of Asia to Hong Kong Tomorrow

It was reported yesterday that Zhang Fakui, the former commander of the Fourth Army, accompanied Wang Jingwei to leave the country, but according to information obtained by this newspaper's reporter from reliable sources, Mr. Zhang did not leave Shanghai yesterday. His relatives and friends held a tea party in a certain place today to see him off. It is heard that Mr. Zhang decided to take the Queen of Asia to Hong Kong on the 24th, stay for a while, and welcome his wife to take the same ship to Europe. Xiao Buyun, Air Force Commander of the Northeastern National Salvation Army, Departed for the United States Yesterday 155

Farewell Banquet Held by the Hongshun Mutual Aid Society the Night Before Last

Xiao Buyun, Air Force Commander of the Northeastern National Salvation Army, has been actively planning all air force equipment since being appointed. He decided to go to the United States to purchase aircraft. He has now purchased a ship ticket through the China Travel Service and will depart on the French mail ship "Andre Lebon" at noon on Saturday. After arriving in Europe, he will transfer to the United States. Ms. Liu Menglian will accompany him. Ms. Liu is going to the United States to study aviation. It is reported that after Commander Xiao's departure, all matters in Shanghai will be entrusted to his secretary, Liu Henwo, and the first team leader, Li Binghui, etc., to handle. It is also reported that Commander Xiao has raised US$140,000 for this trip to the United States, planning to purchase seven of the latest fighter jets first, and then fly to Shanghai and transfer to the Northeast to resist the enemy, with a deadline of no more than two months.

The Hongshun Mutual Aid Society held a farewell banquet at the Red Plum Restaurant the night before last to see off Comrade Xiao Buyun's trip to the United States to purchase aircraft and resist the enemy to save the country. Over fifty people attended, including Yang Wendao, a standing committee member of the Society, all staff members, Mr. and Mrs. Xiao Buyun, and guests Wang Zhiyuan, Pan Yunchao, representatives Wu Gonghu, Huang Yi, Liu Henwo, Huang Yuanbo, Li Binghui, Jiangnan, Lu Mengfei, and others. The chairman, Yang Wendao, delivered a farewell speech. Comrade Xiao Buyun gave a speech about the preparation of the Air Force and expressed his gratitude. All mutually encouraged each other to save the country and resist Japan. The guests and hosts enjoyed themselves until 11:00 PM before dispersing.

Weng Zhaoyuan Hosted a Banquet Last Night 156

The League of Nations Support Association Passes 157

The Implementation of Economic Sanctions Plan

Electing Representatives to Go to the Peking-Shanghai Line to Form Branches

The Municipal League of Nations Support Committee has been actively proceeding since it was initiated by various trade associations. Chambers of commerce from various places have also sent telegrams to join and organize branches. The Association has received letters from the Hangzhou, Jiaxing and Changshu chambers of commerce in recent days, all of which agree to join and actively organize branches. Ke Ganchen, the representative of the Association who went to the Longhai Line to organize branches, also sent a letter yesterday, reporting that he has arrived in Zhengzhou, saying that the chambers of commerce in Xuzhou, Kaifeng, and Zhengzhou have all agreed to join and organize branches. In order to implement economic sanctions against Japan in accordance with the League of Nations covenant, the standing committee meeting yesterday passed the implementation plan. The details are as follows:

Standing Committee Meeting 158

The Association held its fifth standing committee meeting yesterday on the third floor of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce. Over ten people attended, including Luo Qinghua, Jin Runxiang, Zheng Chengqing, Ye Jiaxing, Ge Jechen, and Zhang Peizhen. The following resolutions were passed: (1) Discuss the question of whether the Jiaxing Chamber of Commerce's inquiry about the branch association is an independent nature. It was resolved that the branch association can independently set up a branch office in addition to joining this association. (2) Discuss the case of the chief accountant, Li Wenjie, who resigned due to school. It was resolved that the resignation be approved and Xu Guanqun be promoted to fill the vacancy. (3) Discuss the implementation plan for economic sanctions against Japan. It was resolved to amend and pass it. (4) Discuss the case of representatives going to the Peking-Shanghai Line to contact and organize branch associations. It was resolved that Luo Qinghua, Zheng Chengqing, Ye Jiaxing, Zheng Zenan, Jin Runxiang, Ma Shaoquan, Tu Kaizheng, and Xie Zhongle be elected as representatives.

Telegrams From Various Places 159

The Hangzhou Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Changshu County Chamber of Commerce, and the Jiaxing Chamber of Commerce all sent letters yesterday to join and actively organize branch associations. The Hangzhou Municipal Chamber of Commerce stated in its letter: "In reply, upon receiving your letter and the League of Nations covenant, we have repeatedly reviewed it and found that your association is concerned about the overall situation and is enthusiastic about saving the country, and hopes to resist the enemy's economic aggression with the spirit of peaceful struggle. We admire your painstaking efforts. It has been submitted to the first standing committee meeting of this association, and it has been resolved to reply and agree, and to discuss and proceed with various trade associations accordingly," and so on, and recorded it on file. The Jiaxing Chamber of Commerce and Changshu Chamber of Commerce also sent letters yesterday to join and organize branch associations, the wordy length is omitted.

Letter From Representatives 160

Ke Ganchen, the representative of the Association who went to the Longhai Line, reported in a letter yesterday that he has arrived in Zhengzhou, saying that the Xuzhou Chamber of Commerce has agreed to join, and the Kaifeng Chamber of Commerce, in addition to agreeing to join, has also agreed to convene a joint meeting of the provincial chambers of commerce to notify all chambers of commerce in the province to join together and organize branch associations. The Zhengzhou Chamber of Commerce has also agreed to join.

Fujian People Resisting Imported Goods 166

Two Japanese Warships To Enter Fujian

A certain merchant in this city telegraphed from Fuzhou yesterday that there are again Japanese warships coming to Fujian due to resistance to debt. The situation is recorded as follows:

Workers Refuse to Load and Unload: In the past half month, the dumping of Japanese goods in China has gradually become active again. A lot of goods have also been shipped to Fuzhou. All circles in Fujian Province, seeing the continuous flow of Japanese goods, paid great attention. The loading and unloading workers and barge workers at various wharves agreed to refuse to load and unload. Whenever a Japanese ship arrives in Fujian, regardless of cargo or passengers, they are not allowed to load, unload, carry, or transport on barges. As a result, Japanese ships arriving in Fujian cannot load passengers and goods. The workers also strictly supervise non-Japanese ships to prevent them from being disguised as other ships and smuggled into Fuzhou.

Japanese Warships Summoned to Fujian: Japanese shipping companies in Fujian, unable to operate due to this severe resistance, telegraphed Taiwan to hire Taiwanese coolies and dispatched barges from Shanghai to Fujian to prepare for self-dispatching workers to load and unload. Since the implementation, it has aroused major resistance from the dockworkers and the surface barge gang. Shantou and Xiamen have risen up in response, and the business community has also automatically boycotted. The Japanese merchants went a step further and urgently telegraphed Mawei to dispatch two naval warships carrying a batch of marines to Fujian to demonstrate. They are now arriving in Fuzhou.

The Decline of Japanese Shipping: The Japanese ships sailing from Shanghai to Fuzhou, including the Osaka Company's "Fujian Maru," "Changsha Maru," "Shengjing Maru," and three other ships, have always had a very large business and many passengers. Since the resistance to goods in Fujian, Shantou, and Xiamen, the Japanese ships going to Fujian have no cargo to load, and passengers do not take Japanese ships because they cannot go ashore. In the past ten days, the Japanese ships from this port to Fujian can be said to have no business at all, and only to Keelung do they have a small amount of cargo and passengers.

Xiamen Burned Japanese Goods: Yesterday, a certain merchant received a telegram from Xiamen that recently hundreds of pieces of Japanese goods, such as seafood and kelp, were shipped from Shanghai to Xiamen. They had been transferred from ships to barges and transported into the inner harbor of Xiamen. The matter was discovered by the goods-rejection investigators, who immediately detained the goods and intercepted the barge. They were immediately dragged to the port of Xiamen, and these hundreds of pieces of seafood and kelp and a civilian ship that carried them were burned together as a warning. Now the Xiamen gang has telegraphed to Shanghai, ordering them to pay attention to Japanese goods with changed brands and mixed in for shipment, and the shipping companies have also refused to accept Japanese goods to Xiamen.

Floating corpses are flowing horizontally, heads and flesh are separated, and land and houses have disappeared. The damage from the flooding is difficult to predict at the moment. The cries of the victims escaping and calling for help were heard and seen, and our hearts ached and tears fell. This association responded urgently, rescuing those drowning in the water with boats, and transporting those exhausted on the road with vehicles, and placing them in safe areas from danger. We established six shelters, accommodating more than 20,000 people. More than 30,000 refugees scattered at will, from Xu Gongbei to Jile Temple, sleeping in the open air, eating in the wind, suffering from hunger and cold. More than 30,000 people were given bread and steamed buns twice by this association to alleviate their immediate needs. This is why nearby branches should accept relief funds to help these hungry people. The reputation of the Swastika is at stake. The urgent need for benevolence is urgent. Special report. Binjiang Branch, Jia Yin." Also attached are several copies of the Dalian Swastika Society's remittance of 10,000 yuan for emergency relief and appeals to make the disaster situation clear.

Residents Re-petition the Railway Department Regarding the Site Selection for the New North Station 171

If There is No Approval, Representatives Will Be Sent to Peking

In order to build a new site for the North Station, the Two Routes Bureau has encircled more than 4,000 acres of land in the Zhenru and Pengpu areas. The villagers in the vicinity believe that the railway bureau does not need such a large area to build the station, and only 700 to 800 acres are enough. Therefore, they have petitioned the railway bureau, the Ministry of Railways, and the Municipal Government to reduce the amount of land encircled in order to alleviate the people's hardship. At that time, the Ministry of Railways replied that "regarding the encirclement of land, it cannot be used as a definite method for the railway, because it is still under consideration and there may be changes in the amount of land encircled in the future." However, recently, the Ministry of Railways has increased the encirclement of land by more than 1,000 acres, totaling more than 5,000 acres. The residents of the encircled area are worried about the increase in the encirclement of land by the Ministry of Railways. They first petitioned the Pengpu Municipal Committee Office. The Municipal Committee approved the Municipal Government to handle it with the Ministry of Railways. However, there has been no reply so far. The more than 500 villagers who were encircled now plan to submit a document to the Ministry of Railways first to request relief. If there is no reply, they will send representatives to the Ministry of Railways to petition.

Residents and Shops on North Sichuan Road Petitioned Party and Government Organs Yesterday 172

The Purpose is to Reduce Rent in the War Zone

North Sichuan Road is a place where roads are built beyond the boundary. Since the January 28th Incident, the shops in the area have suffered huge losses due to the impact of the war. After the war, the resumption of business was even more dilapidated. In addition, false alarms were frequent, and people were panicked. The market was no longer as prosperous as it used to be, so the shops were closed one after another, and the rent was so high that it was difficult to maintain and difficult to recover. The citizens in the area went to the 25th Branch of the Citizens' Federation to discuss the matter. After unanimous deliberation, Wei Langxuan, Ye Qichang, Chen Jiufeng, Zhong Peishen, Li Zifeng, Hu Zhaoying, Guan Jichuan, and other seven people were elected to present the shop's account books and the citizens' opinions, and to report the actual situation of business losses. (1) Request the Municipal Government to base the standard for rent exemption in the war zone on the rent starting after the withdrawal of the Japanese troops from District D. (2) Announce that the rent in the war zone must be reduced by 40% to slightly reduce the burden and try to restore the urgent task. (3) Prohibition of eviction and one-sided complaints to the court. They were received by Xiang Weicheng, a member of the Municipal Government, who promised to convey the previous situation to the mayor as much as possible. The representatives then took their leave and went to the Municipal Party Department to petition. They were received by Zhao Erchang, a member of the Civil Training Committee, who described the plight of the war in general. Zhao promised to attach the petitions and various evidence to the Central Government for review and decision, so that they could liberate the citizens. The representatives were satisfied and left at 2:00 PM.

Disputes Over Increased Taxes on Tobacco and Alcohol Licenses 173

Nine Industry Representatives Petitioned Party and Government Organs

Nine public associations in this city, including the tobacco exchange, the sauce and wine sauce encirclement, the restaurant, the dry tobacco, the local yellow wine production, the sorghum shochu industry, the Fen wine, and the Shaoxing wine, elected Chen Liangyu, Zhang Suhou, Qian Wenda, Zhang Dalian, Han Xingwei, Chen Weiwen, Fang Zhongheng, Cheng Kefan, Xie Zhendong, Zhang Songji, Chai Yasheng, and other representatives to gather at the Fumin Road Tobacco Exchange Industry Association at 10:00 AM yesterday. They took two cars to the Municipal Government for a joint petition. At 11:00 AM, the representatives advanced with documents and were received by Section Chief Xu Shaoxiu. The representatives stated that Wang Yao, the contractor of the Shangbao license, was using the police district to assist in implementing harsh harassment and forcing small shops to stamp their seals and acknowledge double the tax payment. If there was any delay, they would be summoned and detained by the police. The small merchants were unable to resist and sent the tax payment to the public association, asking the chamber of commerce to donate on their behalf. The chamber of commerce accepted and handled the matter, but it has not been resolved. Recently, the Shangbao Branch has become even more severe, harassing the chamber of commerce. Members have repeatedly reported that if there is no relief method, they will have to close their business and wait for death. The representatives feared that misunderstandings might occur if this continues, and the expansion of the turmoil would hinder public security. In addition to the actual presentation to the Tax Administration, they specially petitioned your government. Before the deployment is resolved, please order the Public Security Bureau to instruct the various districts not to assist in the harassment for the time being. Section Chief Xu replied that the government and the Public Security Bureau should maintain the duty of maintaining public order with importance to the situation. He immediately instructed the Public Security Bureau not to harass and handle it peacefully. At 11:00 AM, they went to the Municipal Party Department and were received by He Yuanming, who was responsible for mediating the disputes. The representatives said that if they could pay taxes and receive licenses according to the original amount of the Fen wine industry, there would be no problem. Otherwise, they would only ask for a thorough solution. Mr. He agreed to ask the Public Security Bureau not to make things difficult for the time being (the rest is omitted). At 2:00 PM, they went to the Social Affairs Bureau, but the director was out on business. They agreed to meet again on Monday. At 2:30 PM, they went to the Public Security Bureau and were received by Yan Zhizhai from the Second Section. He said that tax affairs are not within the scope of this bureau. The government orders assistance, which is the duty to be fulfilled. Now that your representatives have petitioned the municipal government, they should abide by the order and handle it peacefully, and will not harass or detain. At 3:30 PM, they went to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and were received by Zheng Chengqing. The representatives briefly described the facts of the petition and asked for a fair claim and a letter to the Public Security Bureau to order the various districts to be cautious and peaceful. All tax payments should be handed over to this association for safekeeping, and the deployment should be resolved quietly. Do not be alarmed. The representatives were satisfied and took their leave.

Preparatory Committee for the Chicago Exposition Establishes Sample Collection Offices in Beiping and Hangzhou 176

Branch Offices to Be Established in Hankou, Tianjin, and Other Places

Overseas Chinese Products to Be Sent to the Chicago Review Committee Nearby

The preparatory committee for participating in the Chicago Exposition recently held a committee meeting at the International Trade Bureau to discuss everything. Progress on this matter is currently quite active. The recent developments are divided as follows:

Chicago Organizes a Review Committee. The original rules set by the preparatory office stipulated that all products for exhibition must first be submitted to the office for review and qualification before being selected for display. The committee has now received a request from a majority of overseas Chinese, stating that it is quite inconvenient to transport goods from overseas due to the long distance. Therefore, they requested an alternative method. The committee has now approved this request and decided at a meeting that if any overseas Chinese products are available, they can first contact the committee. However, if it is inconvenient, they may apply to the Chicago committee's review committee nearby for a preliminary review. If qualified, they will be collected and displayed together with domestic products at the exhibition in Chicago.

Sample Collection Offices Established in Beiping and Hangzhou. Beiping and Hangzhou are areas where commercial development and products are concentrated, and transportation is also very convenient. Therefore, the committee has established sample collection branch offices in these locations to collect local specialties. After achieving results, they will be handed over to Shanghai. Currently, sample collection branch offices will also be established in Hankou, Tianjin, and other places.

Preparatory Meeting to Be Held Next Year. The committee originally planned to hold a preparatory meeting in Shanghai before participating in the Chicago Exposition. All products from various parties would be completely gathered in Shanghai, and experts from all walks of life would be invited to provide accurate evaluations, discarding the dross and preserving the essence. Then, they would prepare for all arrangements to participate in Chicago next June, so as to compete with other countries and not lag behind. However, it is reported that funding is currently lacking. The original amount of 400,000 yuan was allocated by the Ministry of Finance, but only 30,000 yuan has been received so far. Therefore, the Ministry of Finance is being asked to find a way.

Public Organizations in Anhui Oppose Grain Tax 177

Telegram to Various Ministries

Anhui Public Organizations' Telegram to Nanjing: To President Song of the Nanjing Executive Yuan, President Shao of the Legislative Yuan, President Yu of the Control Yuan, and Minister Song of the Ministry of Finance: Recently, we read in the newspapers that the Anhui Grain Administration has been established, stipulating a tax of four jiao per shi for rice exported by sail, six jiao for transport by steamship, and three jiao for miscellaneous grains. Li Yunqi, Yu Youquan, and Lu Zhongnong have been appointed as directors of the Wuhu, Bengbu, Dashengguan, and other management offices. After reading this, we are extremely surprised and shocked. The Grain Administration is a disguised form of likin, a transformed version of the grain tax. Last year, Chen Tiaoyuan used the pretext of prohibition to establish this tax. The merchants and people of the entire province unanimously opposed it. An official request was submitted to the National Government, which issued a strict order for its abolition, and the Control Yuan filed an impeachment. Now, Wu Zhongxin, the chairman of Anhui Province, was then a member of the Control Yuan and was particularly critical in reviewing this case. Now that Mr. Wu is in charge of Anhui's administration and it is a time of local decline, he should learn from the past, change course, seek to restore vitality, and relieve the suffering of the people. However, he has violated his original intentions and continued to extract wealth, continuing Chen Tiaoyuan's disastrous policies in Anhui. This is truly unexpected by the people of Anhui. Rice and grain have always been the main agricultural products of Anhui Province, with annual exports of approximately ten million dan, which regulates the province's finances. This year's harvest is abundant, with even more rice in storage. However, due to heavy taxes and merchants' hesitation, rice prices have not improved, directly striking farmers and indirectly causing social panic. The harm is immeasurable. It is also reported that the provincial government has decided to issue 5 million yuan in public bonds, using rice tax revenue as collateral. This action is even more absurd. Not to mention that there is no need for Anhui Province to issue public bonds, and the rice tax is an illegal and exorbitant levy that must be abolished sooner or later. Now, if it is used as a fund to issue public bonds, it is tantamount to forcing the people of Anhui to increase their burden by 5 million, which is illegal and harmful to the people. The people of Anhui will never recognize this. Therefore, we urge your esteemed Yuan to impose strict sanctions and not to approve the issuance of public bonds in Anhui Province. Also, limit Chairman Wu's time to abolish the Grain Administration to maintain the rule of law and relieve the suffering of the people. The telegram is urgent and awaits your orders. Anhui Fellow-Provincials Association in Shanghai, Anhui Students Association in Shanghai, Anhui Public Interest Society, together bow.

Local News II

The Tragic Case at Changchun Tea Garden on North Fujian Road 182

Zhao Xiaowu Secretly Plots to Expose Villains

A Tragic Massacre at Changchun Garden

A tragic case of attempted robbery and assault occurred at the Changchun Baoji Tea Garden at No. 760 North Fujian Road. The details are as follows:

Glimpse of Three People. Zhao Xiaowu, 36 years old, is a local ruffian near the Changchun Tea Garden and a regular customer of the garden. He usually spends his time there, associating with a group of petty criminals and engaging in mischief. Yesterday morning at 10:50, Zhao arrived at the tea house as usual for tea. He saw three people at another table across from him who seemed familiar. He soon remembered that they were his former accomplices in a previous case. He secretly observed their actions and saw that they seemed to be discussing some kind of event. Zhao thought about getting involved, but since he had not greeted them earlier, he was hesitant to speak up. So, he secretly left the garden and went to the Jin Dahua Tea House, where he told Ying Aliuliu and Wang Aqing about the situation and discussed a plan of action. After the three had agreed on a plan, they rushed downstairs and went straight to Changchun Garden.

Shot and Fell to the Ground. On the way, they happened to meet Detective Shang He of the police station. The three told Shang about the situation and invited him to join them. Shang believed that Ying and Wang were his partners, and since they sincerely requested his help, he should lend a hand. So, he followed them. As they approached the Changchun Tea Garden, Zhao Xiaowu stepped forward, followed by Shang, and went straight upstairs. Reaching the tea table where the three were seated, Zhao asked, "Do you know Mr. Shang from the police station?" At the same time, Shang ordered the three not to move. Shang then examined the arm of the person sitting in the middle and saw that the tattoo was still clearly visible. He intended to arrest him on this pretext. However, this person was prepared and, seeing that Shang's expression was not good, quickly pulled out a pistol and fired a shot into the floor to warn them. A group of tea drinkers, hearing the gunshot, immediately ran downstairs in a panic. While they were in chaos, the man fired at Shang. Shang quickly fell backward and was not hit, but the bullet hit Ying Aliuliu, who was standing behind Shang. At that time, Zhao Xiaowu and Wang Aqing were about to run behind the three to grab them, but before they could move, Xiaowu was shot in the back of the head by the man and immediately fell to the ground. Wang Aqing was also shot twice and fell into a pool of blood at the same time.

The Murderer Escaped. The three men, seeing that they had caused a disaster and achieved their goal, took advantage of the confusion to mix into the crowd and escape. By the time the nearby patrol police arrived, they only saw Xiaowu, Aliuliu, and Aqing lying on the ground. They immediately reported to the Old Zha Police Station and summoned an ambulance. They first sent Ying and Wang to Tongren Hospital, and then sent Zhao Xiaowu to Renji Hospital, but he had already died. His body was then transported to the forensic laboratory on Feilun Road for examination. Ying Aliuliu was shot in the chest and lungs, and his injuries were severe. He lives at No. 1922 Gao Lan Lane, Haining Road. Wang Aqing was shot through the left eye, and his left arm was injured. He lives at No. 523 Tangjia Lane. At around 9:00 p.m., Yu A'gen, the chief detective of the Old Zha Police Station, arrested one of the murderers and two women in a lane on Robert Sheng Road in western Shanghai. They also seized three pistols. At 10:00 p.m., they arrested two more women elsewhere. The two murderers who were at the scene are still being pursued.

Hollywood Silver Star 183

Fan Pengke Departs Shanghai

Traveled with President Wang Yesterday

To Hunt Tigers in Sumatra

Hollywood's famous movie star Fan Pengke traveled from the United States to China via Japan for sightseeing. After staying in Shanghai for more than a week, he played golf twice, but unfortunately lost both times. It is reported that after his golf failure, Mr. Fan decided to go to Nanyang to hunt tigers. Yesterday at 11:00 a.m., he boarded the Picture of Fan Pengke on the Anfan Pengke in Shanghai (Photo by Li Zunyong)

De Laipeng French mail ship and left Shanghai to hunt tigers in Sumatra. Mr. Fan traveled on the same ship with Premier Wang Jingwei, who was going to Europe for treatment. He boarded the ship at 10:10 a.m. yesterday. Premier Wang had not yet arrived. The dignitaries who were seeing off Premier Wang were waiting in the cabin on the ship. Suddenly, they saw the movie star they knew so well on the screen, and they all cast curious and warm glances at him. It is currently undecided how long Mr. Fan will stay in Sumatra. According to Mr. Fan, if his wife, Miss Biquefu, still plans to come to China for sightseeing as scheduled, Mr. Fan will also return to Shanghai from Sumatra for a third tour of Shanghai. Mr. Fan wore a brown suit yesterday, and his face was unusually dark, but he was in good spirits.

Han Traitor Zheng Xiaoheizi Arrested in Hongkou 184

Ji Zhongtang Shot to Death by Those People

The Corpse's Mother Reported to the Police Station for Arrest

At the beginning of the Shanghai war, Hongkou, Hujia Muqiao, Xiangyanqiao, and other places were the first to fall, and they were the last to be recovered after the armistice. Therefore, Jiangbei hooligans such as Wang Shubao, Wang Sanshizi, Zheng Xiaoheizi, and others acted as traitors in that area, taking the opportunity to rob and set up opium dens and gambling houses, committing all kinds of evil. Later, Ji Zhongtang, a Jiangbei native who had served as a detective in the Public Security Bureau, was released from the Caohejing Second Prison after being convicted of fraud. He also went to Hujia Muqiao, intending to join their gang and share the spoils. However, due to uneven distribution of the spoils, he was shot and killed by Wang Shubao, Wang Sanshizi, and Zheng Xiaoheizi. At that time, it was still under Japanese military control, so the family managed to transport the body out. After the local court verified the cause of death, it ordered their arrest. Unexpectedly, Wang Sanshizi and Zheng Xiaoheizi have now made countless amounts of money through their evil deeds and have opened tea houses and cigarette shops in Xiangyanqiao. The day before yesterday, they held a birthday celebration for their mother and sent out invitations. The corpse's mother, Ji Wu, learned of this and reported it to the Fifth District Third Precinct, which sent police to the banquet to arrest Zheng Xiaoheizi. The others escaped. After being arrested, he confessed to the previous events. He has been handed over to the Public Security Bureau and then transferred to the local court for prosecution.

Petty Traitor Arrested in Wusong 185

Committed All Kinds of Evil During the Japanese Occupation of Wusong

Yao Lansheng, a local resident of Lijia House on Xi'an Road in Wusong Town, has always been idle and associated with vagrants. During the Sino-Japanese War, when the Japanese army occupied Wusong, he dared to rely on the power of the Japanese to gather gangs to rob people while the local residents had fled. The victims were angry but dared not speak out for fear of being reported to the Japanese army, which would lead to their deaths. Therefore, everyone called him a petty traitor. After the situation calmed down, someone reported him to the Municipal Public Security Bureau. The day before yesterday morning, Chen Caifu and other detectives from the Municipal Public Security Bureau's Detective Team, carrying official documents, came to Wusong and went to the address to arrest Yao Lansheng. On the spot, they found several wool coats, four chairs, and other stolen goods in his house. They immediately took Yao to Shanghai for interrogation.

This Office Orders the Social Affairs Bureau to Investigate and Handle the Taikoo Labor Strike 187

The Social Affairs Bureau Has Scheduled Mediation

Regarding the labor strike of the Changjiang (Yangtze River) route ships of the British Taikoo Company, the Municipal Government yesterday ordered the Social Affairs Bureau to, together with the Municipal Party Headquarters, investigate and handle the matter. It is reported that the Party and government organs have discussed measures and scheduled mediation. The details are as follows:

The Municipal Government Orders the Social Affairs Bureau: The Municipal Government issued an instruction to the Social Affairs Bureau yesterday, stating the following: “In compliance with the matter, we received a letter No. 1706 from the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, regarding the petition submitted by Zhou Xiaoting, representative of the Seamen's Middle Class Guild, and Gao Yongliu, representative of the seamen and middle-class workers of the Taikoo ships, which stated: 'We, the workers, serve on the various ships of the British Taikoo Company, working in the middle class cabins, to make a living. Currently, due to the failure of the compradors of the Changjiang route ships to pursue their selfish interests, they have united and, relying on the power of foreign merchants, are reducing workers and arbitrarily oppressing them. The livelihoods of our thousands of workers are about to be plunged into misery.

Therefore, we specifically submit this petition jointly, detailing the existing improper practices of each ship and the conditions discussed between labor and management. We earnestly request that the China Navigation Mutual Aid Association be ordered to prevent the compradors of each ship from reducing workers, in order to maintain the people's livelihood,' etc. Upon investigation, if the statements in the original petition are true, it is appropriate to forward the order to prevent this, in order to maintain the livelihoods of the workers. Accordingly, we are forwarding the original petition and other documents to your Municipal Government for investigation and handling, and we hope to receive a reply for our review. While the matter was under review, we also received a letter No. 1942 from the Mass Movement Guidance Committee of the Central Executive Committee (excerpt omitted)..." In view of this, we hereby issue this order to your Bureau, instructing you to comply and, together with the Municipal Party Headquarters, investigate and handle the matter thoroughly and report back for review and forwarding. This order." The Party and government have scheduled mediation. After receiving the report, the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau and the Municipal Party Headquarters sent personnel to investigate the truth. Yesterday, they further discussed handling measures and decided that on the 26th, the Social Affairs Bureau would convene a meeting with representatives from the Seamen's Middle Class Guild and the China Navigation Mutual Aid Association to facilitate mediation, in order to prevent the labor strike from escalating and affecting navigation.

Water Police Conference on Winter Defense Escorting Ships 188

Representatives of Various Shipping Companies Convened

Eight Resolutions Reached After Discussion

Zhang Xianyi, District Chief of the Fourth District of the Jiangsu Provincial Water Police, in view of the imminent winter defense season and to prevent robbery cases on commercial ships traveling in the flood areas under his jurisdiction, specifically convened a joint meeting of representatives from the Chongming, Hai, Shanghai, Huguo, and Yang various route shipping companies at the district headquarters at 10:00 AM yesterday to discuss escort measures. District Chief Zhang presided over the meeting. The resolutions are recorded below: (1) Hupu is a place where bandits frequently appear and special attention should be paid. (2) Alarm signs and signals should be handled according to previous cases. (3) Private detectives hired by each ship should contact the detectives of this district (the detectives of this district are based on holding detective certificates with the official seal of the district chief). (4) If any accident occurs to each ship when sailing within the flood season under the jurisdiction of this district, such as capturing bandits, it can be handed over to the patrol ship of each port in this district for delivery to the district. (5) If each company needs official police escort, it can apply to the Civil Affairs Department to order this district to dispatch official police to escort the ship. The escort team is divided into fixed and temporary types. (6) The entry and exit of each ship, and the dates and shifts of loading and unloading, must be notified to the district headquarters in advance during the winter defense period. If there is any change, it must be notified in advance. (7) If private smuggling of firearms and ammunition is found on each ship, the district headquarters should be secretly informed to arrest them. (8) The various cases were discussed and drafted, and the district headquarters printed them for distribution to each representative to take back for reporting. A letter was also sent to the shipping association for reference.

No Parking Zones Along Roads 189

To Be Re-tiled with Black and White Tiles

The Public Works Department's Police Department, because the red paint painted on the roadside in places where vehicles are prohibited from parking is not easy to maintain after various tests, has now tested and changed to laying black and white tiles in each place. Because the black and white are mixed, it is very eye-catching, and the tiles are not easy to be made into the required red color. This matter has been approved by the board of directors, and Articles 28 and 48 of the Traffic Regulations will be amended. The date of implementation will be announced later.

Public Works Department's Fire Department Report for September 194

The Public Concession Fire Brigade responded to 53 fires in September. The most important was the Xinning Shao steamboat. On September 3, a fire broke out in the cotton-loaded cabin on the way to Shanghai. Fortunately, the crew managed to close it tightly. After arriving at the Ning Shao pier, the Central Fire Brigade went by fire boat to rescue it, together with the Chinese Fire Brigade. As a result, only 20 bales of cotton were lost. On the same day, several firefighters were fainted by smoke, and an ambulance was dispatched to rescue them. Unexpectedly, on the way back, they collided with a tram on the Avenue Edward VII, causing eight injuries.

On September 6, the Suiyang ship also caught fire. The ship was going to Wusong to load kerosene to Qingdao. Suddenly, a fire broke out in No. 3 cabin. It retreated to the Taikoo pier in Pudong, and the Hongkou and Central teams went by fire boat to rescue it. After four hours of work, the fire was extinguished.

The fire at Bao Cheng Silver House on Nanjing Road occurred at the end of September. Because the alarm was obviously too late, the fire was already raging when the fire brigade arrived. The houses there were old-fashioned, almost entirely made of wood inside, and there were several patios, so the fire spread very quickly. The Central, Xinzha, and Hongkou teams worked hard to rescue the fire and protect the surrounding houses. As a result, the silver house and the rented restaurants and fruit shops suffered heavy losses. Fortunately, the surrounding areas were spared. More than 80 firefighters worked at the scene.

In total, the property endangered by fire in the concession and special donation areas this month amounted to more than 8 million taels, with an actual loss of more than 149,000 taels. The ambulance team dispatched vehicles 111 times, the hospital team dispatched vehicles 181 times, and firefighters were on duty in entertainment venues for a total of 9,409 hours.

Further News on the Yarn and Cloth Exchange Case 195

The Exchange Discussed the Situation and Settled the Matter

Actually Due to Force Majeure During the Shanghai War

Guo Wen News Agency reports that regarding the contractual disputes between clients Sha Weiyi, Fu Zidong, etc. of the Chinese Yarn and Cloth Exchange, who refused to settle the matter with full price reduction as resolved and announced by the board of directors of the exchange, it was learned that the exchange had already been judged to have lost the case in the First Special District Court. The exchange refused to accept the judgment and appealed. Presiding Judge Hu Yigu accepted the case. As reported in the previous newspaper, the case was still heard in person by Presiding Judge Hu at 1:30 PM the day before yesterday. The lawyers of both parties began to argue fiercely. The appellants Gao Shouting, Mu Xiangyue, Hu Weizeng, and Zhang Binwei of the Yarn and Cloth Exchange were represented by lawyers Liu Chongyou, Zhang Shizhao, Wang Fuchang, and Chen Zhongyin. The appellees Fu Zidong, Sha Weiyi, Wang Junbai, Ming Jingheng, Chen Rongcai, Wang Shengsun, and more than ten other participants, including Wang Guanxian, were represented by lawyers Shi Jiong, Tao Jiachun, Yao Xichen, and Zhang Zhengxue. First, Liu Chongyou, the representative of the plaintiff, stood up to argue, stating that at the time of the Shanghai War, there was force majeure, and the futures trading could not be fulfilled, so it had to be settled. He also presented the government's and various armies' and organizations' declarations and telegrams of long-term resistance. Next, Wang Fuchang made many criticisms of the first-instance judgment, believing that the board of directors of the Yarn and Cloth Exchange had the right to settle on behalf of the clients. Next, lawyer Zhang Shizhao spoke, citing a lot of Chinese and foreign literature, law, and legal studies, mainly that in the 20th century, the individualism of Britain and the United States could no longer exist. Our country's bias towards the administrative nature of the continental policy is not appropriate. The first instance of this case was absolutely individualistic, which is very important to national morality. Moreover, if the exchange could not stop trading at that time, everyone would criticize and condemn it. Therefore, after considering the situation and reasoning, it had to be settled. Moreover, since the Ministry of Industry and Commerce did not take emergency measures, the exchange automatically dealt with it, but was convicted by the society, which is a disgrace to civilized countries, etc. Next, the defendant's lawyer Shi Jiong refuted it item by item. The lawyers spoke in turn, and the debate lasted until after 7:00 PM. Presiding Judge Hu announced the end of the debate and scheduled the judgment for November 2.

Two Robbers Caught One After the Other in Robbery on Xiaoshadu Road 197

At 2:25 AM yesterday morning, when Hua Haishan, the owner of a cigarette and paper shop at No. 886 Xiaoshadu Road, West Shanghai, was fast asleep, two robbers suddenly broke into the shop door and entered the hall. They used guns to prevent Haishan from making a sound and searched everywhere. It happened that Chinese constables No. 2864 and 1088 of the Gordon Road Police Station were patrolling the area and saw that the shop door was wide open, which aroused suspicion. They stepped forward to investigate and saw that the two robbers were searching. The two constables immediately retreated and hid behind a large tree opposite the shop. Before long, the robbers plundered out. The two constables shouted to stop them. Fearing that the robbers would attack, they fired a shot into the sky as a warning. As soon as the robbers heard the gunshot, they ran away. The two constables also started chasing them. On the way, they met two Chinese constables patrolling and passing by, so the four constables joined forces and chased after them. When they were approaching Connaught Road, one of the robbers was captured and a fake pistol and hundreds of copper coins were found on him. The robber was taken to the Gordon Road Police Station. Under interrogation, he claimed to be named Zhang Amao and had an accomplice hiding at No. 421 Chongqing Road. The police station sent detectives to arrest Lu Mulin. The remaining robbers had already escaped after hearing the news in advance. Yesterday morning, the police station sent the two robbers to the court for trial. Because it was still necessary to investigate in detail, the judge ordered the trial to be postponed for a week.

Wang Xiaolai and Wang Yansong Return to Shanghai 199

Optimistic About the Future of the Jiangxi Situation

Wang Xiaolai, Chairman of the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, and Wang Yansong, Executive Committee Member, flew from Shanghai to Xunyang to Nanjing to negotiate with the Jiangxi Provincial Government to abolish production and sales taxes and to investigate Jiangxi's industry and commerce, as leaders of the National Merchant Corps Representatives. They were then summoned by Chairman Chiang and went from Xunyang to Wuhan. They have now returned to Shanghai after completing their official duties. According to them, the banditry in Jiangxi, after being thoroughly suppressed, has been cleared from all places except for a very small part remaining in southern Jiangxi. For example, places like De'an, where travelers could not go before, are now accessible. The municipal administration of Nanchang has also made great progress recently. The cleanliness and spaciousness of the streets are actually better than those of Hangzhou. However, there is a lack of fully equipped hotels, but construction is currently being planned. Jiangxi's finances have always been very difficult. Recently, the central government has defaulted on subsidies, and on the one hand, it has to organize the aftermath of bandit suppression. After the provincial government reorganized tax revenue, eliminated corruption, and reduced waste, it has been able to achieve a balance between income and expenditure. The future of the Jiangxi situation is very optimistic.

The Social Affairs Bureau Instructs That It Is Not Permitted to Privately Examine Weights and Measures 200

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce issued a notice yesterday, saying, "In compliance with Order No. 4637 from the Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, it is for compliance. According to the report from the Municipal Weights and Measures Inspection Office, it is found that various industry and commerce bureaus and industry associations in this city (annually or quarterly have the practice of regularly calibrating the weights and measures used by various colleagues once, but this calibration method, according to the provisions of Article 16 of the Weights and Measures Law, is of an inspection nature and is not allowed to be handled privately by users. Therefore, in addition to ordering each weight and measure manufacturing shop and factory not to privately solicit invitations from various associations to handle calibration work on their behalf, and to be punished for violations, we intend to request your bureau to inform all industry associations that in the future, when calibrating the weights and measures used by various colleagues in accordance with regulations, they must request our office to send personnel to preside over the handling of the calibration before the deadline, and it is not permitted to privately calibrate, in order to emphasize the importance of weights and measures, etc." In view of this, in addition to issuing instructions, it is necessary to notify the association to comply and to inform each industry association separately that in the future, if there are weights and measures instruments to be calibrated by each industry association, they must report to the office in advance and request them to send personnel to preside over the handling, and it is not permitted to privately calibrate, which is necessary, etc." In view of this, we hereby issue this letter for notification and hope that you will check it.

Widow's Family Kidnapped for Extortion Case 201

Accomplice Wang Xunfu Apprehended

Gunshot Wound Still Visible on Wang's Waist

The home of widow Wang Yu, residing at No. 71 Taian Lane, North Shanxi Road, was invaded by many thieves at around 6:00 PM on January 10 last year, who robbed her of property worth more than 300 yuan. When they were about to escape, they kidnapped her for a ransom of 100,000 yuan, agreeing to contact her near North Jiangxi Road on Edouard Road on the 19th of that month. The matter was detected by the police station, which sent Chinese and Western detectives to arrest the thieves. The thieves resisted arrest with gunfire. Two thieves were shot and killed on the spot, and Jiang Dinghui and Wang Xianqiao (also known as Lao Wang) were arrested and sent to the First Special District Local Court for interrogation. Jiang was sentenced to death, and Wang was sentenced to life imprisonment. However, the thief who was looking after the ticket (hostage) had fled after hearing the news, and Ms. Wang also escaped. However, there was still an accomplice in the case, Wang Xunfu from Yangzhou, who was at large. At around 8:00 PM the day before yesterday, Chinese Detective Shen Chongli of the Hongkou Police Station learned that Wang was hiding in a certain number in Yucai Road, Zhabei. He then coordinated with Western detectives and secretly went to the local Public Security Bureau. The detectives arrested Wang at the address and brought him back to the police station. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Local Court. Presiding Judge Shen Bingrong interrogated him. The police station lawyer stated that Wang had previously been shot in the right rib by detectives on Edouard Road, with the bullet entering from the front and exiting from the back. He had confessed to this at the police station. Jiang Dinghui had already been executed by firing squad. The lawyer then ordered the defendant to take off his clothes and show the gunshot wound on his waist, which was clearly visible. Zhang Tianyin, a lawyer from the police station, continued that due to the urgency of the case, the court should temporarily detain the defendant. When questioned, the defendant Wang Xunfu confessed that he had been invited by Jiang Dinghui to rob with five other people. He did not know Wang Xianqiao, who was sentenced to life imprisonment. The rest of his words were evasive. Judge Shen ordered the defendant to be transported to prison and rescheduled the interrogation.

A Man Harasses a Wife and Accuses Her of Extortion 202

Jin Deming, a Jiangbei man who sells tickets for the British and American Tram Company, No. 148, and lives at No. 31 Mattehes Road, was arrested by Chinese Detective Zhang Liang and Western Detective Elder of the Gedeng Road Police Station the day before yesterday for allegedly intimidating and attempting to extort 1,000 yuan from Chen Jikun. He was ordered to be detained. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the First Special District Local Court. According to the police station lawyer Wang Yaotang, the case was stated to be prosecuted in accordance with Article 370, Paragraph 3 of the Criminal Law. According to the victim Chen Jikun, he is a coppersmith in the Public Works Bureau's Motor Vehicle Office. He used to live with the defendant, but now he has moved to No. 72 Xinkang Lane, Xinzha Road. At around 5:00 PM on the 11th of this month, after returning home from work, he passed Mattehes Road and suddenly met the defendant's wife, Jin Guan, who greeted him and said that the light in her home was broken, and asked him to go and repair it. He followed her to her bedroom. Just as he was about to repair it, the defendant suddenly arrived and accused him of harassing his wife, making a lot of noise, intending to extort 1,000 yuan. After negotiation, the defendant wrote a promissory note for 100 yuan and forced him to sign his name and fingerprint on it, and said that if he dared to report to the police station or leak the news, he would be shot with a gun. He was forced by the power of evil and had to agree and retreat. Until yesterday, he suddenly received a threatening letter, attempting to extort 1,000 yuan. He then took the letter and reported to the police station, which sent detectives to arrest the defendant. According to the defendant's wife, Jin Guan, Chen suddenly broke into my bedroom on the afternoon of the 11th, and saw that my husband was not there, so he wanted to force me to do something indecent, and took off his upper body clothes. I refused him, and soon my husband came home and negotiated with Chen. I did not invite Chen to my home to repair the lights, etc. When questioned, the defendant confessed that Chen Jikun was previously my tenant and later moved out. At 5:30 PM on the 11th, I came home and saw Chen and my wife in the room, and Chen's clothes were taken off, and he was wrapped in a blanket, looking very embarrassed, lying in the toilet. I negotiated with him, and he volunteered to write a promissory note for 100 yuan as a settlement. I could only bear it because my family's ugliness should not be publicized. I don't know anything about the threatening letter. This is Chen's fabricated slander. I have been working in the tram company for more than 20 years and have never had any illegal behavior. Now Chen wants to forcibly occupy my wife, but he has fabricated facts to cover up the case. His heart is extremely vicious and should be investigated clearly. He also hired a lawyer to defend him in court. The police station lawyer Wang also said that Chen's teasing was indeed a fact. Judge Ge Cixun checked the confession, ordered the defendant to write numbers in court for verification, and then declared the defendant Jin Deming innocent. He was allowed to post bail and leave the court for instructions during the appeal period.

Xu Zhaohuan Sues His Wife's Family for Inheritance for His Two Sons 203

Xu's Improper Behavior in Court

Greatly Rebuked by the Judge

Lu Xin, the wife of Xu Yongyao, that is, lawyer Xu Zhaohuan, is the daughter of Lu Yunsun. Yunsun passed away in March of the 17th year of the Republic of China. The property he left behind has been distributed equally among his wife and children in accordance with current laws and regulations, and an analysis document has been signed to ensure compliance. However, just three years after Yunsun's death, his daughter Lu Xin also died of illness in December of last year. However, after the death of his wife, Xu Zhaohuan suddenly asked Lu Mingsheng and others to analyze his father-in-law's inheritance, saying that although Lu Xin had passed away, she left behind two sons, the eldest being Weiyuan and the second being Weichong, who should inherit on her behalf according to law. Because the two sons were young, he made a special claim as their representative. However, the Lu brothers refused, causing Xu to sue them in the First Special District Local Court. During the trial, Lu and others hired lawyer Chen Ying to defend them and submitted an analysis document proving the amount of inheritance that Lu Xin had received at that time, which was covered with Lu Xin's seal. Therefore, at the end of the first instance, it was recognized that the plaintiff's lawsuit was completely unreasonable, and the lawsuit was rejected and ordered to bear the litigation costs. Xu was greatly disappointed under the judgment and hired lawyer Lu Qing to appeal to the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court. After a hearing was held once, the hearing was postponed because the appellant requested to add witnesses. Yesterday afternoon, the hearing was continued by Presiding Judge Hu Min of the Second High Court, together with Judges Cai and Lin. The witnesses Lu Qi, lawyer, and Ding Mingquan, doctor, both arrived in court one after another, but most of the appellees did not arrive. First, Ding stated the situation of Lu Xin's medical treatment. Next, Lu Qi stated the characters present at the time of the Lu brothers' property analysis. Lawyer Yan then said that today most of the appellees did not arrive at the building and requested that the witnesses be questioned separately to prevent them from colluding in the future, or that the hearing should be rescheduled until all the appellees had been summoned for the next hearing. The court was deeply dissatisfied with this situation, which was actually delaying the litigation. Unexpectedly, Xu Zhaohuan suddenly stood up and claimed that such questioning could not be considered effective and asked the court not to question any further, saying that questioning was also ineffective. At the time of the speech, he was restless, unsteady in his actions, running around and not paying attention to the order of the court. Presiding Judge Hu was outraged by this strange situation and sternly rebuked him, saying that the purpose of the appellant was purely to focus on money, and he had disregarded the friendship of relatives. Looking at his actions, it can be said that he was blinded by greed, otherwise, how would he dare to make such nonsense, even saying that there was no need to question any further, even if questioning was ineffective, it was to command the judge as a litigant, not only interfering with the trial, he had been a judge for 20 years, and such illegal actions were still a new idea. It is feared that it is not only the case that there are no courts in all of China, but also no courts in Europe and the United States. When the lawyers in the audience heard this, they were all moved, but Xu did not feel it much and frequently claimed that there were still requests, but it was already six o'clock. Judge Zhong ruled that since the appellees had not all arrived, it was difficult to conclude the hearing and ordered that the hearing be continued at a later date.

Murder of Barber Ma Yuangui 204

The Murderer Confesses the Reasons for the Assassination

The Deceased Stole His Funds

And Falsely Accused Him of Having an Affair with His Daughter

Ma Yuangui, 32 years old, a barber from Zhenjiang and a partner in the Ying Ji barbershop at No. 12 Yuxing Street outside Xiaodongmen in the French Concession, was lured out on the evening of the 4th of this month by Ding Mingcai (52 years old), a fellow townsman and barber, under the pretext of going out for fun. In the Yixin Lane of Laoyongan Street, Xiao Famin suddenly attacked, stabbing him six times in the lower abdomen and both arms. He was taken to Renji Hospital for treatment in a police car. At the same time, detectives arrested the murderer in room 37 of the Chunjiang Hotel in Shangren Lane, Wuma Road, in the Public Concession and sent him to the Second Special Court for interrogation and detention. Later, the victim died due to his serious injuries despite medical treatment. The corpse was inspected and identified by the prosecutor, and the corpse's brother, Ma Yuanqing, took it for safekeeping pending review. Yesterday morning, the case was further heard by Wang Gangxu, the chief of the criminal court, in Criminal Division One. First, Gu Shouxi, the police lawyer, explained the case and prosecuted the defendant for causing death by injury. Then, Detective Zhou Buguang reported the investigation process after the incident and the circumstances of the defendant's arrest. Then, the deceased's brother, Ma Yuanqing, stated that his brother had been brutally murdered and requested justice. He also said that his brother left behind a widow who is now pregnant and about to give birth, and a six-year-old child. He requested compensation of 200 yuan for funeral expenses and 5 yuan per month for ten years for the child's education, totaling 600 yuan. Ding Mingcai confessed that the deceased and he jointly opened the Shanhaitang barbershop at No. 23 Bulao Sibi Street, Xueyueli, Vladivostok, in 1919, each contributing 200 yuan. The deceased monopolized the management. In 1928, he dismantled the partnership due to losses, and the defendant was reimbursed 40 yuan. Later, the deceased stole 200 Japanese yen and 40 US dollars and came to Shanghai. He wrote a letter to the defendant's son-in-law, Li Deming, saying that the defendant had an ambiguous relationship with his daughter. The son-in-law sent his wife, the defendant's daughter, back to his home and did not want her anymore, and also wrote to scold the defendant. Later, the deceased tried to rape the defendant's daughter, causing the defendant's wife to become ill with anger and resentment. For this reason, the defendant hated him to the extreme and killed him, and is now willing to plead guilty. The court verified the confession, but since the deceased's wife had not arrived, it ordered a postponement for further interrogation. The defendant was returned to custody, and the deceased's brother was instructed to bring the deceased's wife to court for verification next time.

Murder Caused by Buying Toilet Paper 205

Originated from Defecation

An old man named Yang Yonglin, who lived in Hujia Muqiao, Hongkou, went to the grocery store opened by Lu Zihuai early the day before yesterday morning to buy a piece of toilet paper for defecation. Two Accidents Involving China General Omnibus Yesterday 206

Damaged a Rickshaw The China General Omnibus tram, No. 48 on the Third Circle Road, with license plate No. 7, driven by driver No. 86, was traveling from Ximen along the right side of the track near Minli Middle School at 1:33 pm yesterday when a rickshaw carrying two female passengers suddenly pulled onto the track. The tram driver injured his left hand. The police arrived and took both parties to the First District Headquarters for investigation.

Blind People Gambling by Shaking Dice 207

Spectators Could Not Help But Smile

Feng Zhong, an old woman from Ningbo and the hostess of Feng Tianxing's fortune-telling house at No. 130 Lafayette Road in the French Concession, was recently in financial difficulties and unable to make ends meet. She had a whimsical idea and invited ten blind people from the same industry the day before yesterday evening, including Han Longtai, Zhu Ahong, Dong Jintang, Zhang Aqing, Xu Qihao, Chen Qingjia, Ni Rongchang, Yu Yiwan, Yuan Gengsheng, and Weng Chengfang. Seven sighted people, including Zhu Aqing, Wang Akang, Sun Wenrong, Zhou Baoxing, Weng Yunchun, Li Zisheng, and Wang Mingjin, led them to the back hall of her house. The ten blind people gathered together to gamble by shaking dice, hoping to earn a commission. The sighted people called out "Green Dragon, White Tiger, Enter Treasure" from the side. They started gambling at around 10 pm and gambled until 3:10 am in the morning. Just as they were having a great time, the incident was discovered by the gambling squad of the French Concession Police. Chief Detective Li Yousheng, Deputy Detective Liu Kunbao, and Detectives Xiang Rongji, Xu Wenshao, and Zhang Dongcheng, along with Western Detective Ali Cai (transliteration), quietly went to the scene, first guarding the front and back doors, and then knocking on the door. They rushed in to search. Unexpectedly, the blind people, upon hearing the knocking sound, became anxious and came up with a plan. They immediately hid the dice and gambling money in their mouths or shoes, and used the dice shakers as teacups, pretending to be discussing business matters with their colleagues. However, everyone looked flustered. After repeated questioning by Detective Li and others, they discovered the flaws. They dug out four dice from the mouths of the blind people, including Han Longtai, and found more than 30 silver dollars, 247 copper coins, and four lottery tickets. They took them to the police station. After questioning by the police chief, he ordered the head to be detained, and each gambler was released on bail with a cash deposit of five yuan. At that time, only Zhu Aqing, Han Longtai, Wang Akang, Zhu Ahong, Dong Jintang, Zhang Aqing, and Xu Qihao were detained due to lack of funds. Yesterday, they were escorted to the Second Criminal Division of the Second Special Court for investigation. When the bailiffs led the defendants to the courtroom, the blind people supported each other and walked in file, causing the spectators to smile. Everyone said that since the defendants were all proficient in fortune-telling, why didn't they each predict in advance that they would not fail? During the conversation, Yao Zhaodi, the police lawyer, explained the case and said that the defendants had committed the crime of gambling and requested that they be interrogated according to law. Feng Zhong confessed that she had gathered for gambling due to temporary financial difficulties, which she did not deny. Han Longtai all admitted to being gamblers. Judge Wu Fanglian verified the confession, announced the end of the debate, and adjourned for sentencing at a later date.

Huafeng Transported and Sold Corrosive Liquid 208

Spilled on the Ground, Affecting Pedestrians

Huafeng Paint Store in Xinbeimen transported two wooden boxes of corrosive liquid, a total of four large barrels, to Minxin Chemical Plant on Oujia Road, Hongkou. Yesterday (22nd) at around 11:00 am, they hired a small iron-wheeled vehicle pulled by a local man named Tao He. While traveling near the intersection of Sichuan Road and Wuma Road, for some reason, the corrosive liquid they were carrying spilled on the ground, boiling and giving off a foul odor along the way. At that time, Yu Apin, who lived at No. 3 Huachang Lane, Beiqiujiang Road, was knocked to the ground by Zhu Xie Lin's bicycle. His clothes were corroded by the chemical, and many other pedestrians were knocked down by rickshaw No. 8566. The clothes they were wearing were all turned to powder. Many coolies stepped on the corrosive liquid, and their skin was immediately corroded, causing them to scream in pain. The order was greatly disrupted. The Global Automobile Company located there sent people to wash the road with tap water to avoid accidents. The damaged pedestrians all went with the rickshaw puller Tao He to Huafeng Paint Store to negotiate a settlement.

Fire Alarm on North Fujian Road 209

At 5:50 pm yesterday, a fire suddenly broke out on the upper floor of the reception room in the warehouse of Huaying Pharmacy at No. 491 Zhidian Lane, North Fujian Road. At that time, the old clerks were having dinner downstairs. Seeing the flames bursting out of the upstairs window, they rushed upstairs in a panic, only to find that the fire had already broken through the roof. They hurriedly ran out of the alley to call for help. The patrol police reported to the Central Fire Brigade, which immediately rushed to the scene to put out the fire. By 6:30 pm, the fire had been extinguished. Only the reception room on the upper floor of the house was destroyed, so the loss was light. Only a few boxes of medicines were rendered useless after being wetted. The four neighbors in the area were slightly alarmed but suffered no losses.
