The Shanghai Lixiao Association convened a meeting of the leaders of its 72 subordinate public offices yesterday, with 84 people attending. Election Minutes of the Merchant Ship Officers Association 212

The China Merchant Ship Officers Association, due to the successive re-election of executive committee members, lacked restrictions, and the right of election of a group of members seemed to be biased and withered. In this election, the new regulations were specially amended, and the original executive members were first drawn by lot, with two people being drawn each year to stop re-election in order to increase the opportunity for other elected members to serve as executive members. The two people who were drawn this time were Chen Ganqing and Yang Zhixiong. The results of the association's election a few days ago were that Huang Xiaohan, Jin Yueshi, Wu Jinxiang, Shen Jiyun, Ma Jiajun, Zhu Zhe, and Huang Junxiang were elected. Among them, Jin Yueshi and Shen Jiyun applied for resignation because they each held positions in the shipping industry and found it difficult to juggle both. According to the regulations, Sha Xiangjia and Jia Dingxi, who had the next most votes, were appointed as replacements. On the same day, a meeting was held to discuss the method of recovering pilotage rights, the preferential treatment of foreign crew members by shipping companies, discrimination against Chinese crew members, and many other important motions. Due to the time of publication of this session, it will be kept secret for the time being.

Letters to the Editor 225

To the Editor: Upon examining your newspaper's local news column on October 21st, an article titled [Negotiations Between Taikoo Company and Union Fail] stated that Xie Baosheng and others from the China Shipping Mutual Aid Association held four direct negotiations on September 26th, 29th, October 4th, and 14th. After reviewing this negotiation, I have not yet been informed, nor have I attended. What your newspaper published, I think it is rumors untrue, especially sent the letter for corrections, to show the facts. This to Shen Bao, Xie Baosheng, sealed, October 22,

Reading your newspaper on the 22nd, in the local news, it mentioned the cracking down of the Communist Party organs in Ningbo Road, which stated that on the top floor of Qian Xinglong Grocery Store at No. 236 Chongde Lane, the intersection of Ningbo Road and Shanxi Road, a distribution department of the Jiangsu Provincial Committee of the Communist Party was set up to hide and operate, etc. After investigating, our store has nothing to do with this, and the door number is also wrong. Our store is No. 136. On that day, the top floor of No. 137 next door did have a crackdown on the Communist Party situation. It must be a false inquiry. I sincerely fear that outsiders will not know the truth, and the reputation of our store is at stake. I especially sent a letter to your newspaper, quickly making corrections, hoping for this. This to the Editor of Shen Bao, Qian Xinglong Yangtie Company, sealed, October 22, 21st year

Nine Three Elder Ma Xiangbo's Sayings

Nurturing Children and Respecting Women 226

— Jing · Recorded ·

Elder Xiangbo sometimes strolled along the corridor in front of the Leshan Hall, slowly walking and looking at the flowers displayed on both sides; several times I heard Elder Xiangbo admire the beauty of the flowers, and even more praised the supreme goodness of the Creator: originally, the wealth and glory that enjoyed great fame in ancient times and scattered all over the ground are not as good as a fresh lily with complete color, fragrance, and taste in the field!

I remember once, Elder Xiangbo specifically pointed to a flower tree and said: [Take a closer look!] I paid close attention and watched for a while: the newly grown tender leaves are always well protected. From this, we can see the wonder of creation, telling people: nurturing children is the natural duty of the family; because children who cannot be independent, if they are not properly protected and educated, will be like those tender leaves that are not well protected, either dying prematurely or losing their beauty!

Next was the problem of [managing the family]. Elder Xiangbo quoted the Book of Changes sequence diagram, saying that there are men and women, there are husbands and wives, and then there are fathers and sons, accumulating into a family. He also spoke about respecting women from a doctrinal perspective. Jing notes: Min Yi Chen Shoufan's translation of [Training of National Character of European and American Powers] contains a passage that can be quoted to verify Elder Xiangbo's words. (See page 70 of the Commercial Press edition.) [All European and American countries know how to respect women: because doctrine declares that all personalities are equal before the Creator; and because of respect for the Virgin Mary, there is no base psychology of playing with ordinary women. Medieval knights paid more attention to this level. Afraid to follow each other, become customs, go out by car, but also give way to women. I should also improve customs ｜ At least in the family, the patriarch should abide by the [Father's Way] and [Husband's Way]; never arbitrarily scold his wife and daughter, often causing family tragedies! This is the first step in so-called [family management].]

[The Way of Husband and Wife] 227

— Bi

丨Three Chapters of Outline丨

In this day and age, divorce is nothing more than the most fashionable thing. To open the skylight and speak frankly, divorce is nothing more than the most tragic thing. A husband cannot do without a wife, and a wife cannot do without a husband, like a person looking for food, and there is seven or eight points. Divorced husbands and divorced wives each regain their freedom, indeed getting what they want. But after divorce, everything inevitably feels unusually empty, and emotions feel particularly depressed, like the same person suddenly being unemployed, like to the extreme.

Working as a shop assistant, if your temper is bad, you will lose your job. Husband and wife often quarrel. Fights inevitably lead to divorce. Divorce is as painful as unemployment. Therefore, to not divorce, one must only abide by the [Way of Husband and Wife]. What is called the [Way of Husband and Wife]? Listen to me tell you.

If a husband has a lover, or a wife has a lover, the other party must not be jealous. Just go outside and find a lover yourself, each doing their own thing. This is the first chapter of the [Way of Husband and Wife]. If one party is drinking, watching dramas, gambling, or messing around outside, the other party must not pull a long face and admonish them, just follow suit and mess around outside. When the money is spent, they will naturally stop. This is the second chapter of the [Way of Husband and Wife]. If one party suddenly loses their temper, scolds a few times, and hits a few times, the other party must not retort or retaliate. When one party's anger subsides, then scold a few times and hit a few times in the same way. Although this is a revenge movement, both sides can understand each other. This is the third chapter of the [Way of Husband and Wife].

The above three chapters are just an outline of the [Way of Husband and Wife], but they have summarized the essence of the [Way of Husband and Wife] without leaving anything out. If you all recognize that divorce is a modern thing, and that not divorcing is not fashionable, then please do as you please. If you also say that divorce is painful, then please study the above three chapters. If you can put them into practice, I dare say that the old man in the divorce court will be dozing off, and the lawyers will have to give up their careers and change jobs.

Standards for Modern Women in Choosing a Spouse 228

— Huang Yingdai

丨The New Concept of "Marrying a Daughter a Cut Above"丨

In China, men and women have always been extremely unequal. In the eyes of most people, there is a deep-rooted concept of favoring men over women. Even when parents choose a spouse for their daughter, they always hold the prejudice of "marrying a daughter a cut above." In terms of wealth and reputation, the man's family must always be somewhat superior to the woman's family. Under such circumstances, in society, class boundaries are very clear in marriage. Young people from the proletariat absolutely have no possibility of marrying wealthy young women.

In recent years, superficially, women in general seem to have become more self-aware. The wave of the women's movement has spread throughout the country. The slogan of equality between men and women has become a tired cliché. However, from what we see in reality, where is there equality between men and women? A very high barrier still stands between them, because women themselves mostly hold a mistaken view, believing that they are inherently inferior to men in terms of strength, thus causing the prejudice of favoring men over women to continue to be passed down in Chinese society. Even in terms of marriage, although modern women in general have broken the concept of "marrying a daughter a cut above," in their minds, the spouses they choose do not necessarily have to have more wealth or reputation than the woman's family.

However, they still hold the old prejudices regarding academic qualifications: a woman who has graduated from elementary school must at least marry a man who has graduated from junior high school; junior high school graduates must marry high school graduates; high school graduates must marry college graduates; after graduating from college, they will only marry those who have studied abroad; if they cannot find someone who has studied abroad at a higher level, they have to settle for marrying a fellow returnee. If they do not fit these criteria, they would rather not marry and embrace singlehood. Under these circumstances, it is evident that women still acknowledge their weakness compared to men and want to rely on men for life. What is the difference between this and the former concept of "marrying a daughter a cut above"?

Time After Marriage 229

— Ms. Lüzhu

丨All Spent on the Child丨

When a person is in her maiden days, which dreams of the future are not splendid and extraordinary? But what is the result? Mostly disappointment! Believing that life after marriage is far from as ideal as in maidenhood, resulting in disappointment and frustration, and from frustration to a little discouragement!

In reality: maidenhood is a woman's golden age, making us always cherish the memorable past. I have now changed from a maiden to a young married woman. I can only ponder the past; I can only imagine the future; I am just at a loss for the present!

Before, I thought that after marriage, I could manage the household chores while still reading and studying, and then spend my free time chatting and laughing with my husband to relieve loneliness. Who knew that after getting married, I have to get up early in the morning to tidy up the room, buy vegetables, and cook. In the afternoon, there are still a lot of needlework and many miscellaneous things. There is simply no time left; moreover, now I have a child to feed, hold, and take care of. I am so busy! How can I still touch books? My husband cannot always come home often because of his job. Even if he does come home, he is worried about firewood, rice, oil, and salt. The so-called chatting and laughing can only be sought in dreams!

Most of the reduction in my happiness after marriage is due to economic pressure, and a small part is due to the entanglement of household chores. Fortunately, my husband is exceptionally considerate of me. Although we lack material enjoyment, we still have spiritual happiness. I am also very happy to have adopted a child. Although I usually feel disgusted when I see urine and feces, I don't feel that my child is dirty at all. Although I have to change dozens of diapers a day, I don't feel bothered because I think, "It should be so." When I have free time, I play with my child, and I find it particularly interesting. My days after marriage are spent like this!

Ideal Husband 230

— Rui Yucheng

丨A Typical Male丨

He grew up in a countryside rich in natural beauty; he is the son of a farmer, but he has received a considerable education. He is the most gentle, the most handsome, the most sincere, the most affectionate, the most noble; a person who is sound in both body and mind.

His gentleness is not weakness, nor is it cowardice; he is like a ray of sunshine after a long spring rain, shining on people, making them feel bright everywhere and happy everywhere.

His handsomeness is not decoration, not clothing; he is born with a great physique, dark skin, strong muscles, and an agile and healthy spirit, so people feel that he is beautiful in every way. His sincerity is not hypocrisy, not stubbornness; what is in his heart is what is in his attitude; regardless of joy, anger, sorrow, or happiness, everything is a pure expression of his inner self.

His affection is permanent and unchanging; I remember when I had smallpox, he took care of me day and night; after smallpox, my face was scarred, but he still loved me as before.

His nobility is natural and subjective; once, the daughter of Wang the Millionaire and the younger sister of Chairman Li tempted him with love, but he rejected them all. He said: "The most valuable thing in life is dedicated love."

His body is very strong; he has never been sick. He can ride horses, play ball, swim, and race.

His knowledge is very accurate; he can write, compose, paint, and sing.

He has lived in my heart since childhood, and his virtues and talents have also gradually grown day by day. I cannot forget him for a single day, hour, minute, or second.

However, where is he now?

New Women's Virtues 231

— Huang Wenhao

Chinese daughters are indeed Europeanized now. What we see every day are creatures with curled hair, painted eyebrows, outlined eyes, dyed lips, and protruding chests and buttocks, active in the world. I translated a piece of writing about women's virtues to offer before Mrs. Indamore: Excessive decoration of clothing is enough to prove that you do not understand the true meaning of beauty. Every time a new fashion becomes popular, you should pay attention to whether it suits your personality. Blindly following is not acceptable. Do not wear faded, stained, or other unclean clothes in the home. At the breakfast table, you should wear clean and bright clothes, because it can bring an indescribable joy to the whole family.

Fresh air, moderate exercise, and a balanced diet can give you natural beauty. Material cosmetology is enough to cover your true beauty.

A gentle voice is a recognized virtue.

Kissing is common in social situations, but be cautious. Before understanding your friend's attitude, keep romantic terms as far away as possible in your conversation. Otherwise, the word "Dear" will be followed by the word "Detestable."

On a bus or tram, if someone gives you a seat, do not forget to thank them. It does not cost you much, but the reward the other person receives can be felt. Do not open your small umbrella in crowded places or place it at the entrance or exit.

If two men are walking together, and you are standing in the middle, you should hold both of their arms or neither of them.

When you are hosting a banquet, you should pay attention to the number of guests invited. It should not be too many, because it is easy to have problems such as inadequate care, slow service, and inability to fully enjoy the event. Do not suspect that a friend's attitude towards you is different because you were not invited to a banquet this time. In fact, they also have other friends, and it is not convenient for you to gather together at the same time.

When a friend shows you a newly bought item for you to see, you should not say: "It's too expensive. I would never pay that price." This unintentionally implies that your friend was foolish to pay so much. Do not ask your friend how much the new clothes they are wearing cost. When you know that your friend is starting to read a novel, do not tell them the content and nature of the book in a self-righteous way, because you can reduce their interest in the book, and the author of the book can tell them more than you can.

When you meet friends, do not praise how clever and cute your children are, otherwise, it will cause your friends to feel uncomfortable. When your husband comes home tired from work, do not bother him with trivial matters in the family. You should smile at him.

Do not leave the bedroom before your hair is styled, and do not go outside wearing casual clothes.

Do not criticize the servants in front of your husband. If you have something to say, you may as well wait until he has left.

Treat your husband, do not be attentive one moment and indifferent the next, because living together is forever!

Do not neglect your husband because you have children.

Make sure that your husband can always see lively children and a clean house when he comes home.

After marriage, continue to love your husband with the same attitude as at the beginning, and this will show your sincere character.

Do not use household expenses to buy your personal clothes and accessories, and do not wear torn clothes in front of your husband.

Supplement to the *Shen Bao* Local News

Speech

Liang Zuoyou and Zhang Zongchang the Buddha 232

—

Regarding Liang Zuoyou's donation of wealth to save the country. I made a categorical statement in my previous commentary, that Liang definitely would not have such a large sum to rescue the country, because I have never seen a wealthy person who does not seek fame. Yesterday, I saw a report that a certain celebrity in Tianjin had sent someone to Huang County to secretly investigate and found out that Liang's family was poor, with only half an acre of land, and they relied on a younger brother to help them make a living. Liang had a good friend, A, who was an adjutant following Zhang Zongchang. In 1927, when Zhang failed, A carried a suitcase to Liang's house, claiming to be going to Dalian. Unexpectedly, A went out to visit friends and never returned. Liang opened the suitcase and found more than a hundred foreign bank checks, worth more than 30 million yuan. Liang was afraid of getting into trouble and kept silent. After Zhang was assassinated, he planned to donate the money to the National Government. This situation may have happened. Then it is clear that the money was not Liang's.

However, there are still several points of doubt. (1) When Zhang Zongchang was in Shandong, he must have had many trusted followers. Why would he entrust the important value of more than 30 million to an adjutant who was a follower, and not send a trusted person to accompany him? (2) Zhang had been in Shandong for a long time, and the adjutant's relatives and friends must have been numerous. Why would he hand over the suitcase to a poor scholar? (3) Why did the adjutant go out to visit friends and never return? These are the three points of doubt. In addition, there are two other points of doubt. Zhang Zongchang lost such a large sum, did Zhang not mention it? Why did no one know? It is suspected that Zhang had savings in a foreign bank. I do not know the rules for depositing money in foreign banks, but if a check is lost, is there no other way, such as declaring it lost, to recover the deposit? That is doubt number two. Assuming that there are other ways to retrieve it, then this kind of check is as good as waste paper. The check is already a bounced check and can hardly be cashed. These points are my hypothetical doubts and are not worth mentioning.

In short, this statement is still close to the truth, because only Zhang Zongchang would have such a large fortune, and only this kind of unclear money would be donated in such a large amount of 30 million. Assuming that this matter is indeed true, I cannot help but have a feeling that Zhang Zongchang extorted the people's wealth in Shandong, leaving no stone unturned. Zhang spent money like water and was quite generous. Just taking his concubines as an example, it was said that he had as many as twenty-six at the time (currently there are still fifteen who are said to be being dismissed). The extent of his extravagance can be imagined. And Zhang still had a huge sum of more than 30 million deposited in a foreign bank. May I ask where this kind of huge sum came from? It was nothing more than accumulated wealth from extorting the people's fat and cream. It is clear that it was money acquired through sin.

The *Book* says, "Wealth acquired through immoral means will also be lost through immoral means." Zhang Zongchang's lifetime of wealth acquired through sin, I do not know what karma caused it to fall into the hands of Liang Zuoyou, and I do not know what karma caused it to be transferred to the country. Zhang Zongchang probably did not expect this in any way. The saying goes, "Life and death are destined, wealth and honor are in the heavens." Money obtained through robbery by any means is always unreliable. It is not only Zhang Zongchang who is like this. Since the Republic of China, the money of warlords has either been seized by others or disputes have arisen due to unequal distribution of spoils. This has already been seen many times. Several warlords should also have some awareness of this and stop desperately extorting to fill their own pockets! Lord Mengchang said that accumulating wealth to leave to descendants is not knowing who they will be, and neglecting public affairs will lead to daily losses. It can be seen that in ancient times, accumulating wealth to leave to descendants was not worthwhile. Now people actually want to accumulate money for Zhang San, Li Si, Wang Wu, and Zhao Liu. It is really foolish.

Science

Mineral Fertilizers: Superphosphate and Chilean Saltpeter 234

— Sheng Zhanneng

Superphosphate and Chilean saltpeter are both major nitrogenous fertilizers that can supplement the deficiency of animal and plant fertilizers, and their efficacy is faster than that of natural fertilizers, so this is of great benefit to agriculture. In our country, which is based on agriculture, special attention should be paid to this. I will discuss them separately below:

(1) Superphosphate

Superphosphate is a kind of artificial fertilizer or chemical fertilizer. In recent years, the superphosphate imported into Shanghai and major commercial ports is mostly the "Crescent" brand of the British firm Brunner Mond & Co. and the "Lion and Horse" brand of the German firm Eilisse & Co. In addition, the "Nine Bulls and Two Tigers" brand of the Chinese firm Zhaofeng Co., the "Man and Lion" brand of the New Construction Company, and the "Elephant" brand of the Linong Fertilizer Company are also very well-known. In addition, there are various other brands of superphosphate, totaling no less than thirty or forty kinds, which shows the wide application of superphosphate. Although the materials and ingredients of superphosphate are different, generally speaking, they are nothing more than ammonium sulfate, potassium sulfate, sodium nitrate, and superphosphate.

The properties of superphosphate Superphosphate is rich in nitrogen, phosphorus, and potassium (the three elements of plants), while natural fertilizers (that is, self-supplied fertilizers) contain very little, so its efficacy is very fast. However, natural fertilizers are rich in organic matter, which promotes the vigorous development of microorganisms and gradually improves the soil quality, while superphosphate does not contain organic matter, so if it is not mixed with natural fertilizers, the soil quality is very easy to deteriorate.

The application of superphosphate Our country's farmers are not used to using superphosphate, so caution should be taken when applying it. First, the type must be identified, and attention should be paid to the amount and method of application, because although superphosphate has a fast effect, if it is applied excessively, it often makes the solution in the soil too thick and alkaline or acidic, which damages the plants. The most reasonable application is to use self-supplied fertilizers such as compost, manure, and green manure as the main fertilizer, and then add superphosphate to supplement the deficiency of the three elements to maintain soil fertility. What should be paid most attention to is that superphosphate should not be used as a base fertilizer, but only for topdressing, and it must be applied in several times.

(2) Chilean Saltpeter

Chilean saltpeter is a natural mineral fertilizer produced in mineral deposits with scarce rainfall in Chile, Peru, and other parts of South America. The crude ore contains 17-75% sodium nitrate, the rest being sodium chloride (table salt), sodium sulfate, calcium sulfate, magnesium sulfate, potassium sulfate, etc. Therefore, the crude ore after mining must be refined before it can be used. The refining method is to first crush the crude ore, place it in a large tank, and heat it with water, so that the ore dissolves. After cooling, the insoluble matter settles to the bottom of the container. Chilean saltpeter is stored in the solution and can be transferred to another tank and exposed to sunlight to evaporate and crystallize. The product obtained by this method contains more than 90% sodium nitrate, which is the Chilean saltpeter currently sold on the market.

The properties of Chilean saltpeter Usually, Chilean saltpeter contains about 15-15.5% nitrate nitrogen, which is easily soluble in water, so plant roots can absorb it immediately, but its properties are extremely hygroscopic and have a tendency to solidify the soil and deteriorate the soil quality, so it should not be used in paddy fields, because not only can it be lost with drainage, but the nitrate in it is also easily reduced and transformed into nitrite, which is harmful to plants. Chilean saltpeter has a great effect on dryland crops, even exceeding superphosphate.

The application of Chilean saltpeter Chilean saltpeter is easily dissolved by rainwater and lost, so it should be applied in several times according to the soil quality and crop type. The best time to apply it is when plants are growing vigorously. If it is applied in winter or when plant growth is slow, the effect is minimal. Chilean saltpeter is a simple nitrogen fertilizer, so it must be mixed with phosphorus fertilizer and potassium fertilizer (which should be slightly acidic, because Chilean saltpeter is a physiologically alkaline fertilizer), but it should not be mixed with plant-based organic fertilizers. If it is unavoidable or necessary, you must also choose fully decomposed ones to prevent nitrate from being reduced. This kind of natural mineral fertilizer is most suitable for vegetables, tea, mulberry, indigo, and other germination fertilizers. Each acre can be applied with 15 to 20 catties (Chilean saltpeter easily absorbs moisture, so it should not be exposed to the air, but should be stored in a sealed container to prevent deliquescence).

Society Improvement Discussion Group

From the Issue of School Fee Payment to the Restoration of Labor University 235

— Wen Bing

In the column on the 14th, there was an article [Discussion on the Issue of School Fees]. After careful reading, it can be seen that the author has a lot of good intentions. The whole meaning is to painfully point out the badness of the current commercialization of education, so it is necessary to rectify the fee payment in order to achieve the popularization of education and the rationalization of fee payment. Although this is a pertinent statement of the current abuses, it is impossible to break through the barriers of reality. Why? Please briefly state as follows:

Due to the impact of foreign capitalism, the current Chinese society is moving step by step towards the capitalist ladder. The large cities have already taken shape. Generally speaking, the events in this kind of society have been commercialized. This is the first difficulty caused by reality. Most of our country's universities are gathered in cities. Urban life is expensive. Rent, equipment, and everything else cost a lot. This is the second difficulty. In today's chaotic society, it is not easy for intellectuals to find employment. Most of them can only start schools to find a way out. Therefore, most school founders not only rely on this to maintain their own livelihoods, but also to support their families. There is no other way. This is the third difficulty. Based on these three reasons, the education in our country is becoming increasingly aristocratic, and the methods of collecting fees are increasing day by day. If we only talk about rationalizing the fee payment and popularizing education in this way, it is difficult to achieve in reality. This is why I believe that the theory of a certain gentleman cannot be accepted by ordinary schools at present and can only be achieved in the future society.

But if so, should we not seek another way out? That is definitely not the case! I mean, we can only appropriately increase the education funds in the national treasury, and set up more public schools. In other words, all the party and government officials should quickly realize this, slightly reduce the production of artillery fire that kills their own people, as well as take fewer concubines, buy fewer cars, and prepare their own planes, and transfer the funds to start schools. The most important thing is to restore Jiangwan Labor University.

Labor University was established in 1927, reduced in scope last autumn, and closed down this summer. The treatment of the school was the best in the country. Tuition and food were free. Not to mention, even the students' accommodation during the winter and summer vacations was provided by the school, and there were also uniforms and books to be distributed. In the five years of operation, the students benefited greatly, and the society was even more affected. It is a memorable page in the history of education in our country. It is a pity that the former president, Yi Peiji, managed the school loosely, resulting in few significant achievements, which angered the authorities. Later, Wang Jingqi, a diplomat, took over, but there were repeated disturbances, which led to the closure of the school. Many poor young people wept and hung their heads and were forced to leave the school. This cannot be said to be a fundamental bankruptcy of education in our country, and the authorities intentionally assassinated the youth!

Since the school was closed, there have been many people who coveted to share the large amount of school property left behind, but because of the public's attention, they have not dared to implement it openly for a while. However, if this continues for a long time, even if there is a school property management committee, it will definitely be difficult to avoid being eaten away and gradually become nothing.

Therefore, the restoration of Labor University is an urgent task for the education community in our country, and it is also possible in reality: First, the school property is still there and there is a foundation. Second, restoration is much easier than creation. Moreover, in terms of the social needs of this kind of education, it is even more urgent.

In my opinion, the restoration steps are as follows: (1) Appoint an educator to organize a restoration committee. (2) Appoint a pure educator as the president of the school. (3) Thoroughly liquidate the school property. (4) Repair the part of the school building that has been destroyed by Japanese slaves' artillery fire. (5) Determine the fundamental policy of labor education, with the cultivation of productive technical talents as the main goal, and the management of labor production social talents as the secondary goal. (6) Prepare to restore the school and recruit students. What needs to be paid special attention to here is that the students recruited must be truly poor and unable to attend school.

Last week, the newspaper reported that the education authorities had a restoration plan and that Chu Minyi would be appointed as the president. If this is truly sincere, then the restoration of Labor University may be hopeful, and the flower of labor education may reappear in our desolate society. I hope that our news media and social figures will jointly promote it! What I have said here is just an [index].

School Photo 236

In the University 237

— Hengyu

During the first week of classes at ××× University, only foreign professors started teaching on time. The rest began teaching in the second week, with several announcements posted, all saying the same thing: "××× will officially begin classes next week." Afterward, what one often encountered was occasionally going to the school and finding a notice saying: "Professor ××× has an engagement today and will be absent for one day." Thus, people would come from afar only to make a wasted trip. Professors who didn't want their salaries docked came up with the method of making up the classes, which was good, preventing students from losing out on their studies. However, whether students are free during the make-up time is a question. In theory, teachers can make up for classes, and students can also ask teachers to make up for missed classes. I suspect that this may be the way things are done by Professors.

The staff gentlemen are very pretentious, thinking they are ×× chiefs. When you go to ask them about something, they always ignore you, unless it involves money coming in. Just talking about completing enrollment procedures, students had to run to them almost every day for a week after the start of school.

The library is about the same size as the reception room of a shikumen house, displaying a few large dictionaries and magazines and newspapers. There are very few books on academic research. When A class is in session, students taking B class have nowhere to rest and can only gather there to drink tea and chat. The quiet and silent library has turned into a noisy teahouse.

Classes have started. Professor ×, carrying a few hardcover Western books, strides into the classroom very impressively, like turning on a gramophone. He recites a few sentences from his bag of tricks and lectures on a few paragraphs. The students below seem to be listening quietly, but in reality, the boys are sketching his portrait on their notepads, and the girls are writing small notes and passing them around. Finally, Professor × asks: "Any Question?" He senses no response, so he dismisses the class ten minutes before the bell rings. Such tedium makes the wealthy patrons who paid the tuition for this course unhappy to study.

Professor C, in the first class, announced the textbook to be used: "My Textbook is ×××××, the cheapest book for this course, priced at ten × yuan × jiao." After paying fifty or sixty yuan in tuition, there are still forty or fifty yuan in book fees, lecture fees, and miscellaneous fees. Universities are truly made of money. The children of the poor are not welcome. Whether one can find a job paying thirty or forty yuan after graduation is probably still a question.

So-called university education is really like this!

A Corner of Society

Husband and Wife's Argument 238

— Wu

Mr. Lin was evicted from his house by the second landlord half a month ago. Until today, his entire family has been staying at a friend's house. Originally, this was a very embarrassing thing because bothering people is always uneasy, especially since even the friend is now moving, and he hasn't found his own house yet. Of course, we can imagine how anxious he is. So, he finally discussed it with his wife:

"Hey, we have to find a house today no matter what."

"But where can we find one? A front and back building costs at least twenty yuan, which would take up most of our living expenses, and less than two rooms isn't enough to live in. So, you want it cheap, big, and clean at the same time, so where are you going to find it?"

"But you have to find it, you can't just keep leeching off your friend, can you?"

"Then you go find it, I can't find it."

"Me go find it? Look how shabbily I'm dressed. Before I even walk in the door, the landlords will size me up, either telling you first thing, 'The rent here is very high,' or bluntly replying, 'Already rented out.' As for a man renting a house, they'll ask, 'Do you have a family?' That's simply out of the question, so it's more convenient for you to go."

(Don't tell me I'm not shabbily dressed?)

"But you still have a silk cheongsam, which can at least get you by. Me, in this lined robe that looks like it was dug out of a coffin, I look like a little beggar."

"Don't be so fussy. We're not comparing clothes right now. You have to go once too."

"Sigh, you always get angry when you say that… If there's no way, just rent something a bit more expensive."

"Hahaha, you're just saying things irresponsibly, so full of hot air, you're really a big-eyed pauper. I ask you, if we live in such an expensive house, what will you use to buy rice? What will you use to pay the nanny's wages? It's easy for you to say, but you're so old, you simply don't think things through."

"But, Madam, we have to move out tomorrow, so what else can we do?"

"Then you go try. I've really run around enough in the last half month. It's like 'three pennies for a bowl of soy milk, wanting it full and hot.' I really can't handle this impossible task."

In the end, Mr. Lin dusted off his clothes and shamelessly went to look. Mrs. Lin watched his thin and hunched back disappear.

Finally, Mrs. Lin sat down on the edge of the bed, feeling very distressed. She thought:

"There are people here without houses to live in, while some houses are empty with no one living in them. It's really too unreasonable." She cursed modern society, certain that only with a thorough reform of the current society could one live comfortably.

Market News 239

Wuzhou Holds One-Yuan Group of Gu Ben Soaps: Wuzhou Gu Ben Soap Factory, located in Xujiahui, Shanghai, produces various soaps of excellent quality, strong fragrance, and beneficial to the skin. Patriots all like to buy and use them. Recently, to revitalize national goods, the company specially produced a large batch, holding a one-yuan group soap sale. Each group contains more than twenty bars and sells for only one yuan. The Wuzhou Pharmacy main store on Fourth Horse Road and all Wuzhou branches in the city are simultaneously distributing them and welcome everyone to visit,

Old Shanghai Cooperative Society Catalog Published: The Old Shanghai Consumer Cooperative Society, located at No. 14, first floor, No. 3 Museum Road and Tilanqiao in the city, recently compiled and printed the first issue of a special discount factory store catalog, which has already been published. It includes twelve stores such as Taikang and Chen Jiageng on Nanjing Road. All members and non-members can obtain it nearby.

Welcome from Academic Circles, Female Students]: [Female Students] pictorial weekly, edited by Wu Chengda, has been very well received by academic circles since its publication. The sixth issue will be published this Saturday, with news from dozens of schools such as Guanghua, Daxia, Fudan, Zhongxi, and Qixiu. All newspaper vendors have retail sales. A trial copy is available with a one-dime postal charge. Five issues sent together. The address of the society is the Green Light Publishing House, Penglai Market, West Gate.

Gu Ji'sheng Public Expense Payment Case (Main Text) The defendant shall pay the plaintiff thirty yuan in public expenses. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant. ▲Plaintiff, that is, Counter-Defendant Li Shifu v. Wang Yongkang et al. Debt Case (Main Text) The plaintiffs et al. shall equally compensate the plaintiff silver one thousand one hundred and six taels and five mace. The counterclaim of the defendants et al. is dismissed. The litigation costs of this trial and the counterclaim litigation costs shall all be borne equally by the defendants et al.

Jiangsu High Court Second Branch 243

Criminal Judgments In the case of Zuo Qiaosheng regarding his wife, Zuo Ji'shi's, offense against public morals (Main Text) The original judgment is revoked. Zuo Ji'shi, that is, Zuo Ji'shi, is sentenced to two months of imprisonment for assisting in enticing a girl under the age of sixteen to commit adultery with another person. The number of days of detention before the judgment is determined will be deducted from the imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. ▲In the case of Tan Fucai for injury (Main Text) The appeal is rejected. ▲In the case of Sun Hongqing for murder and robbery (Main Text) The appeal is rejected. ▲In the case of Shen Yitai for knowingly purchasing stolen goods (Main Text) The appeal is rejected.

Civil Judgments Yiyu Company v. Taoyuan Restaurant Rent Arrears and Eviction Appeal Case (Main Text) The appeal and the request for provisional execution are both rejected. The second instance litigation costs shall be borne by the appellant. ▲Innovation Construction Factory v. Taihe Foreign Firm Goods Payment Appeal Case (Main Text) The original judgment is altered. The appellee's claim is rejected. The first and second instance litigation costs shall be borne by the appellee. ▲He Jinlin v. Hengfeng Yonghao Debt Appeal Case (Main Text) The appeal is rejected. The second instance litigation costs shall be borne by the appellant. ▲In the case of Sun Jingwen v. Zhao Shoumin Debt Appeal Case (Main Text) The appeal is rejected. The second instance litigation costs shall be borne by the appellant. ▲Fan Lushi et al. v. Huang Genji, that is, Huang Genmei Land Rent Appeal Case (Main Text) The original judgment is altered, except for ordering the appellant Huang Genji to hand over the land to the appellant Fan Lu et al. for repossession. The house built by the appellant Huang Genji, located in Nianzi Xu, Public Concession Da Tong Road, Mei Xing Li, Shangyi 27th Bao 10th Tu, shall be handed over to the appellant Fan Lushi et al. for transfer of ownership and to compensate the appellant Fan Lushi et al. for losses of silver dollars one thousand and forty-one taels, six mace, and seven fen. The appeal of the appellant Huang Genji and the remaining appeals of the appellant Fan Lushi et al. are rejected. The first and second instance litigation costs shall be borne by the appellant Huang Genji. ▲Fan Lushi et al. v. Huang Genji Land Rent Appeal Case Request for Provisional Attachment (Main Text) After the petitioner provides a security deposit of two thousand yuan, the rent of the house built by Huang Genji in Meixingli, Datong Road, may be provisionally attached. (The above is dated October 22nd)
